🎯

本周核心方向（ML × ferro / 凝聚态）

3 篇

新材料方面，自旋-1/2 kagome 海森堡反铁磁体在磁场中展现出 m=1/3、5/9、7/9 的稳健磁化平台，由√3×√3晶胞的平移对称破缺稳定；更具争议的 m=1/9 平台则呈现两种竞争的价键晶体态，均具有3×3晶胞并同时破缺平移与点群对称。新方法方面，视觉变换器神经量子态（ViT-NQS）被成功用于 kagome 反铁磁体的变分研究，而物理信息神经网络（PINN）通过三级损耗优化求解一维耦合电弹动力学系统，位移和电势的全局相对L2误差分别为2.34%和4.87%。新现象方面，二维铁磁伊辛模型的结构复杂度Cₛ在临界温度Tc处出现显著峰值，该指标基于无损图像压缩对晶格配置的柯尔莫哥洛夫复杂度进行近似，并通过与像素排序/随机打乱配置的可压缩性比较实现归一化，表明信息论度量可作为与模型无关的关键性敏感探针。

  1. 01
    自旋 1/2 kagome 海森堡反铁磁体磁化平台的变分研究：来自视觉变换器神经量子态的方法
    Variational study of the magnetization plateaus in the spin-1/2 kagome Heisenberg antiferromagnet: an approach from vision transformer neural quantum states
    🎯 核心📖 arXiv

    📄 摘要：arXiv:2602.12998v1 发布类型：新 摘要：我们分析了自旋 1/2 kagome 海森堡模型在磁场中的磁化曲线。使用基于神经网络的最先进的变分波函数，我们确认在饱和值的 m=1/3、5/9 和 7/9 处存在鲁棒的磁化平台，并通过 sqrt3× sqrt3 晶胞的晶格平移的自发对称破缺来稳定。关于更具挑战性的 m=1/9 平台，我们发现了两个竞争的价键晶体，具体取决于系统尺寸，它们都破坏了平移和点群对称性，并且具有更大的 3× 3 晶胞。这种具有磁化平均值局部调制的量子态可以在不久的将来通过实验观察到。

    📐 方法要点：采用视觉变换器神经量子态（ViT-NQS）作为变分波函数，研究自旋-1/2 kagome海森堡反铁磁体在磁场中的磁化曲线。

    🔗 相关工作关联：延续了神经网络量子态在量子磁性中的应用，特别是针对kagome晶格中高度阻挫基态的长程关联与对称破缺问题。

    💡 对你方向的启示：m=1/9平台的两种竞争价键晶体态具有可观测的磁化平均值局部调制，为实验探测提供了明确的量子态特征。

    阅读原文 ↗
  2. 02
    寻找铁磁体中的混沌边缘：通过图像压缩量化 2D Ising 相变的“复杂性”
    Finding the Edge of Chaos in a Ferromagnet: Quantifying the "Complexity" of 2D Ising Phase Transitions with Image Compression
    🎯 核心📖 arXiv

    📄 摘要：arXiv:2602.15185v1 公告类型：新 摘要：动力系统中存在的“复杂性”的数据驱动表征仍然是一个在物理科学领域广泛应用的开放性问题。我们研究了二维铁磁伊辛模型的“结构复杂性”，这是一个在特定临界温度下表现出二阶相变的范例系统，通常被引用为复杂形态的典型例子。我们通过算法信息论的视角，通过标准无损图像压缩算法近似晶格配置的柯尔莫哥洛夫复杂度，定义了这种结构复杂性的定量度量mathcal Cₛ。我们通过将配置的可压缩性与其按像素排序和随机打乱的对应配置的可压缩性进行比较来规范我们提出的指标 mathcal Cₛ。我们得出 mathcal Cₛ 的定义，作为分别代表系统偏离完美有序和无序的两个分量的乘积，然后将其绘制为温度的函数。我们的数值模拟揭示了已知临界温度 T_c 下 mathcal Cₛ 的明显峰值。这一结果表明，此类信息论测量可以充当敏感的、与模型无关的关键性指标，直接量化有序与混沌之间边界处复杂结构的出现，为无法获得分析解决方案的领域中的数据驱动应用程序打开大门。

    📐 方法要点：以无损图像压缩算法近似晶格配置的柯尔莫哥洛夫复杂度，定义并归一化结构复杂度指标Cₛ。

    🔗 相关工作关联：连接了算法信息论与统计物理中的相变研究，拓展了信息论度量在临界现象表征中的应用。

    💡 对你方向的启示：Cₛ在Tc处的显著峰值证明，无模型依赖的信息论指标可直接、敏感地标识临界性。

    阅读原文 ↗
  3. 03
    使用三级损耗优化对耦合电波和弹性动力波传播进行建模的统一物理信息神经网络
    A Unified Physics-Informed Neural Network for Modeling Coupled Electro- and Elastodynamic Wave Propagation Using Three-Stage Loss Optimization
    🎯 核心📖 arXiv

    📄 摘要：arXiv:2602.13811v1 公告类型：cross 摘要：物理信息神经网络在 SciML 中提出了一种新颖的方法，该方法通过损失函数中的软约束将偏微分方程形式的物理定律直接集成到神经网络中。这项工作研究了 PINN 的应用来求解一维耦合电弹动力学系统，该系统对应力-电荷形式的线性压电进行建模，由弹动力学和电动方程控制。我们的模拟采用前馈架构，将时空坐标映射到机械位移和电势。我们的 PINN 模型的位移和电势的全局相对 L2 误差分别为 2.34% 和 4.87%。结果验证了 PINN 作为耦合瞬态偏微分方程系统的有效无网格求解器，尽管在耦合特征值系统中的误差累积和刚度方面仍然存在挑战。

    📐 方法要点：构建统一的前馈PINN架构，通过三级损耗优化求解一维耦合电弹动力学（线性压电）的瞬态偏微分方程组。

    🔗 相关工作关联：将物理信息神经网络从单物理场扩展至机电耦合的多物理场问题，属于科学机器学习中的无网格求解器探索。

    💡 对你方向的启示：验证了PINN对耦合瞬态PDE系统的求解能力，但耦合特征值系统中的误差累积与刚度问题仍需克服。

    阅读原文 ↗
01

本周总览#

先把握一周的主线，再进入交叉重点与专题全文速览。

整体概览

本周共137篇文献，其中铁电/磁性91篇、AI/ML 50篇。铁电/磁性领域以交替磁性（altermagnetism）、莫尔量子材料中的拓扑相变、低维磁性及自旋电子器件为主；AI/ML方面则聚焦于机器学习原子间势（MLIP）、物理信息神经网络（PINN）及量子启发的张量网络方法在材料模拟中的加速与扩展应用。

趋势观察

交替磁性（altermagnetism）持续高热，从RuO₂基态争议、CrSb能带分裂到altermagnet结输运和约瑟夫森偶奇效应，理论与实验并进。莫尔量子材料中，压力/电场调控的连续拓扑相变和陈绝缘体-莫特绝缘体转变成为核心前沿。低维磁性方面，应变工程（Ca₂RuO₄、Janus石墨烯纳米带、h-FeS）被广泛用于调控磁序、居里温度和拓扑输运。AI/ML在材料科学中深度渗透：MLIP从零样本预测走向主动学习和多尺度耦合，PINN/神经算子加速复杂PDE求解，量子启发方法（张量网络、混合量子经典网络）开始展现独特优势。

后续展望

altermagnetism的实验确证与器件应用、莫尔材料中拓扑相变的原位调控将是下一阶段重点。MLIP与实验数据的闭环结合，以及量子计算方法在更大尺度材料模拟中的实用化，有望显著加速新材料发现。

交叉研究#

优先覆盖 AI × 物理 / 化学 / 材料的直接交叉工作。

01

高质量 SrRuO3 (111) 薄膜中固有的低自旋态和应变可调的反常霍尔缩放#

Intrinsic low-spin state and strain-tunable anomalous Hall scaling in high-quality SrRuO3 (111) films

AI 解读：该研究通过机器学习辅助分子束外延制备出超高质量的SrRuO₃(111)薄膜，残余电阻率比达该取向最高值。核心创新在于首次系统揭示了(111)取向下外延应变可调控反常霍尔效应的内在与外在贡献比例，并证实

阅读原文 ↗
页内定位所在专题
中文摘要

arXiv:2602.15361v1 公告类型：新 摘要：(111) 取向的 4d 铁磁钙钛矿 SrRuO3 (SRO) 提供了独特的三角晶格几何形状，使其成为探索贝里曲率驱动和自旋轨道耦合输运的有前途的平台。在这里，我们对通过机器学习辅助分子束外延在 SrTiO3 (111) 基板上生长的厚度 t = 1.2-60 nm 的高质量 SRO (111) 薄膜的结构、磁性和磁输运进行了系统研究。我们在 60 nm 厚的薄膜中实现了 45.5 的残余电阻率比，这是该方向报道的最高值，从而能够获得固有的电子和磁性行为。与温度相关的电阻率证实了相干应变 (t = 10, 20 nm) 和应变松弛 (t = 60 nm) 薄膜中 15 K 以下的费米液体输运，从而实现了详细的磁输运和磁测量。线性、非饱和正磁阻持续高达 14 T，而霍尔效应测量和温标将异常霍尔效应的内在 (Karplus-Luttinger) 和外在 (侧跳) 贡献分开，相对重量由 (111) 外延应变调整。 Ru M2,3 和 O K 边缘的 X 射线磁性圆二色性以及 SQUID 磁力测量表明，相干应变和松弛薄膜都具有本质上低自旋的 Ru 基态，解决了先前报告中的歧义。这些详细的晶体、电学和磁学特征为理解和设计 SRO 中的量子传输提供了严格的基础 (111)。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.15361v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: The (111)-oriented 4d ferromagnetic perovskite SrRuO3 (SRO) offers a unique triangular-lattice geometry, making it a promising platform for exploring Berry-curvature-driven and spin-orbit-coupled transport. Here, we present a systematic study of the structure, magnetism, and magnetotransport of high-quality SRO (111) thin films with thicknesses t = 1.2-60 nm grown on SrTiO3 (111) substrates by machine-learning-assisted molecular beam epitaxy. We achieved a residual resistivity ratio of 45.5 in a 60 nm-thick film, the highest reported for this orientation, enabling access to intrinsic electronic and magnetic behavior. Temperature-dependent resistivity confirms Fermi-liquid transport below 15 K in both coherently strained (t = 10, 20 nm) and strain-relaxed (t = 60 nm) films, thereby enabling detailed magnetotransport and magnetic measurements. The linear, non-saturating positive magnetoresistance persists up to 14 T, while Hall-effect measurements and temperature scaling separate intrinsic (Karplus-Luttinger) and extrinsic (side-jump) contributions to the anomalous Hall effect, with the relative weight tuned by (111) epitaxial strain. X-ray magnetic circular dichroism at the Ru M2,3 and O K edges, together with SQUID magnetometry, demonstrates an intrinsically low-spin Ru ground state for both coherently strained and relaxed films, resolving ambiguities among prior reports. These detailed crystalline, electrical, and magnetic characterizations provide a rigorous foundation for understanding and engineering quantum transport in SRO (111).

02

从经典到量子：扩展 Prometheus 以无监督地发现三维和量子系统中的相变#

From Classical to Quantum: Extending Prometheus for Unsupervised Discovery of Phase Transitions in Three Dimensions and Quantum Systems
📚 arXiv👤 Brandon Yee, Wilson Collins, Maximilian Rutkowski📅 2026-02-17⚡ 磁性/铁电🤖 AI/机器学习
AI 解读：该工作将无监督相变发现框架Prometheus拓展至三维经典与量子多体系统，核心创新在于提出量子感知VAE（Q-VAE）以处理复值波函数与量子涨落，实现了三维Ising临界指数的高精度提取及量子临界点
arXiv:2602.14928v1 公告类型：新 摘要：我们将用于无监督相变发现的 Prometheus 框架从 2D 经典系统扩展到 3D 经典和量子多体系统，解决了更高维度的可扩展性和量子涨落的泛化问题。对于 3D Ising 模型 (L łeq 32)，该框架检测文献值 0.01% 以内的临界温度 (T_c/J = 4.511 ± 0.005)，并以 ≥ 70% 精度提取关键指数 (β = 0.328 ± 0.015, γ =…
阅读原文 ↗
页内定位所在专题
中文摘要

arXiv:2602.14928v1 公告类型：新 摘要：我们将用于无监督相变发现的 Prometheus 框架从 2D 经典系统扩展到 3D 经典和量子多体系统，解决了更高维度的可扩展性和量子涨落的泛化问题。对于 3D Ising 模型 (L łeq 32)，该框架检测文献值 0.01% 以内的临界温度 (T_c/J = 4.511 ± 0.005)，并以 ≥ 70% 精度提取关键指数 (β = 0.328 ± 0.015, γ = 1.24 ± 0.06, ν = 0.632 ± 0.025)，通过 ḩi² 比较 (p = 0.72) 正确识别 3D Ising 普适性类别，无需分析指导。对于量子系统，我们使用复值波函数和基于保真度的损失开发了量子感知 VAE (Q-VAE) 架构。应用于横向场 Ising 模型，我们在量子临界点检测中实现了 2% 的精度 (h_c/J = 1.00 ± 0.02)，并成功发现基态磁化强度作为序参数 (r = 0.97)。值得注意的是，对于无序横向场 Ising 模型，我们检测到以激活动态缩放 łn ξ sim |h - h_c|⁻ψ 为特征的奇异无限随机临界性，提取与理论预测一致的隧道指数 ψ = 0.48 ± 0.08 (ψ = 0.5)。这表明无监督学习可以识别不同类型的关键行为，而不仅仅是定位关键点。我们对经典热转变（T = 0 到 T > 0）和量子相变（T = 0，变化 h）的系统验证表明，基于 VAE 的发现可以推广到根本不同的物理领域，为探索分析解决方案不可用的相图提供了强大的工具。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.14928v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: We extend the Prometheus framework for unsupervised phase transition discovery from 2D classical systems to 3D classical and quantum many-body systems, addressing scalability in higher dimensions and generalization to quantum fluctuations. For the 3D Ising model (L łeq 32), the framework detects the critical temperature within 0.01% of literature values (T_c/J = 4.511 ± 0.005) and extracts critical exponents with ≥ 70% accuracy (β = 0.328 ± 0.015, γ = 1.24 ± 0.06, ν = 0.632 ± 0.025), correctly identifying the 3D Ising universality class via ḩi² comparison (p = 0.72) without analytical guidance. For quantum systems, we developed quantum-aware VAE (Q-VAE) architectures using complex-valued wavefunctions and fidelity-based loss. Applied to the transverse field Ising model, we achieve 2% accuracy in quantum critical point detection (h_c/J = 1.00 ± 0.02) and successfully discover ground state magnetization as the order parameter (r = 0.97). Notably, for the disordered transverse field Ising model, we detect exotic infinite-randomness criticality characterized by activated dynamical scaling łn ξ sim |h - h_c|⁻ψ, extracting a tunneling exponent ψ = 0.48 ± 0.08 consistent with theoretical predictions (ψ = 0.5). This demonstrates that unsupervised learning can identify qualitatively different types of critical behavior, not just locate critical points. Our systematic validation across classical thermal transitions (T = 0 to T > 0) and quantum phase transitions (T = 0, varying h) establishes that VAE-based discovery generalizes across fundamentally different physical domains, providing robust tools for exploring phase diagrams where analytical solutions are unavailable.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.13811v1 公告类型：cross 摘要：物理信息神经网络在 SciML 中提出了一种新颖的方法，该方法通过损失函数中的软约束将偏微分方程形式的物理定律直接集成到神经网络中。这项工作研究了 PINN 的应用来求解一维耦合电弹动力学系统，该系统对应力-电荷形式的线性压电进行建模，由弹动力学和电动方程控制。我们的模拟采用前馈架构，将时空坐标映射到机械位移和电势。我们的 PINN 模型的位移和电势的全局相对 L2 误差分别为 2.34% 和 4.87%。结果验证了 PINN 作为耦合瞬态偏微分方程系统的有效无网格求解器，尽管在耦合特征值系统中的误差累积和刚度方面仍然存在挑战。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.13811v1 Announce Type: cross Abstract: Physics-Informed Neural Networks present a novel approach in SciML that integrates physical laws in the form of partial differential equations directly into the NN through soft constraints in the loss function. This work studies the application of PINNs to solve a one dimensional coupled electro-elastodynamic system modeling linear piezoelectricity in stress-charge form, governed by elastodynamic and electrodynamic equations. Our simulation employs a feedforward architecture, mapping space-time coordinates to mechanical displacement and electric potential. Our PINN model achieved global relative L2 errors of 2.34 and 4.87 percent for displacement and electric potential respectively. The results validate PINNs as effective mesh free solvers for coupled time-dependent PDE systems, though challenges remain regarding error accumulation and stiffness in coupled eigenvalue systems.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.12998v1 发布类型：新 摘要：我们分析了自旋 1/2 kagome 海森堡模型在磁场中的磁化曲线。使用基于神经网络的最先进的变分波函数，我们确认在饱和值的 m=1/3、5/9 和 7/9 处存在鲁棒的磁化平台，并通过 sqrt3× sqrt3 晶胞的晶格平移的自发对称破缺来稳定。关于更具挑战性的 m=1/9 平台，我们发现了两个竞争的价键晶体，具体取决于系统尺寸，它们都破坏了平移和点群对称性，并且具有更大的 3× 3 晶胞。这种具有磁化平均值局部调制的量子态可以在不久的将来通过实验观察到。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.12998v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: We analyze the magnetization curve of the spin-1/2 kagome Heisenberg model in a magnetic field. Using state-of-the-art variational wavefunctions based on neural networks, we confirm the presence of robust magnetization plateaus at m=1/3, 5/9 and 7/9 of the saturation value, stabilized by a spontaneous symmetry breaking of lattice translations with a sqrt3× sqrt3 unit cell. Regarding the more challenging m=1/9 plateau, we find two competing valence bond crystals depending on the system size, both breaking translation as well as point group symmetries and with a larger 3× 3 unit cell. Such quantum states with local modulations of the magnetization average values could be observed experimentally in the near future.

页内定位所在专题
中文摘要

克服钙钛矿-钙钛矿异质结在同时提高内置电势和抑制非辐射复合方面的固有局限性仍然是钙钛矿太阳能电池的一个关键挑战。在这里，我们介绍了一种基于铁电的异质结架构，它通过协同机制解决这一双重挑战。首先，铁电异质结固有的自发极化显着放大了内置电场，增强了电荷分离和传输，从而将开路电压从1.16 V提高到1.21 V。其次，铁电核通过溶解-再结晶调节有效调节钙钛矿结晶动力学，有效抑制陷阱态并将填充因子从83.6%提高到86.8%。冠军器件的功率转换效率为 26.62%（认证为 26.07%），开路电压填充因子积为 1.05 V，达到 Shockley-Queisser 极限的 90.3%。此外，改进后的器件表现出增强的运行稳定性，在最大功率点跟踪 500 小时后保留了超过 85% 的效率，为高性能光伏电池绘制了清晰的路径。

English Abstract

Overcoming the inherent limitations of perovskite-perovskite heterojunctions in simultaneously boosting built-in potential and suppressing non-radiative recombination remains a critical challenge in perovskite solar cells. Here, we introduce a ferroelectric-based heterojunction architecture that addresses this dual challenge through synergistic mechanisms. Firstly, the spontaneous polarization inherent to the ferroelectric-based heterojunction significantly amplifies the built-in electric field, enhancing charge separation and transport, thereby increasing open-circuit voltage from 1.16 to 1.21 V. Secondly, ferroelectric nuclei effectively regulate perovskite crystallization kinetics via dissolution-recrystallization modulation, effectively suppressing trap states and elevating fill factor from 83.6% to 86.8%. The champion devices achieve a power conversion efficiency of 26.62% (certified 26.07%) with an open-circuit voltage-fill factor product of 1.05 V, reaching 90.3% of the Shockley-Queisser limit. Furthermore, the modified devices demonstrate enhanced operational stability with over 85% efficiency reservation after 500 h of maximum power point tracking, charting clear pathways towards high-performance photovoltaic cells.

[原始信息] Nature Communications, Published online: 18 February 2026; doi:10.1038/s41467-026-69391-3 Wu et al. report a strategy of incorporating either Dion-Jacobson phase or Ruddlesden-Popper phase ferroelectric perovskite with FAPbI3 to form bulk heterojunctions, increasing the open-circuit voltage-fill factor product and enabling single junction solar cells with an efficiency of 26.62%.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.15126v1 公告类型：新 摘要：RuO₂ 已被提议作为一种典型的金属 d 波交替磁体，一种 Néel 有序补偿反铁磁态，表现出非相对论动量相关的自旋分裂；然而，它的磁基态在理论和实验上仍然存在争议。通过全面的第一性原理计算，我们研究了具有 (110)、(100) 和 (001) 取向的 RuO₂ 薄膜，这些薄膜都是独立式的和支撑在 TiO₂ 基板上的。我们表明，RuO₂ 薄膜中的磁性非常脆弱，受到应变、表面取向和原子弛豫的强烈影响，同时对布里渊区积分方案的选择也高度敏感。尽管拉伸应变会产生有限的磁矩，但所研究的系统都没有稳定补偿的反铁磁状态。因此，无法实现交变磁基态。相反，磁响应的特点是明显的层和位点相关变化和不完整的力矩补偿，类似于亚铁磁状态。我们的结果调和了相互矛盾的理论和实验报告，并强调了 RuO₂ 磁性对结构和方法细节的敏感性。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.15126v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: RuO₂ has been proposed as a prototypical metallic d-wave altermagnet, a Néel-ordered compensated antiferromagnetic state exhibiting nonrelativistic momentum-dependent spin splitting; yet, its magnetic ground state remains controversial both theoretically and experimentally. Using comprehensive first-principles calculations, we investigate RuO₂ thin films with (110), (100), and (001) orientations, both freestanding and supported on a TiO₂ substrate. We show that magnetism in RuO₂ thin films is highly fragile, strongly influenced by strain, surface orientation, and atomic relaxation, while also being highly sensitive to the choice of the Brillouin-zone integration scheme. Although tensile strain induces finite magnetic moments, none of the studied systems stabilizes a compensated antiferromagnetic state; hence, an altermagnetic ground state cannot be achieved. Instead, the magnetic response is characterized by pronounced layer- and site-dependent variations and incomplete moment compensation, resembling a ferrimagnetic-like state. Our results reconcile conflicting theoretical and experimental reports and underscore the sensitivity of RuO₂ magnetism to structural and methodological details.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.15131v1 公告类型：新 摘要：Altermegnets 是一类以自旋分裂电子带为特征的金属磁体。使用 ARPES 方法、磁输运和扭矩测量，并结合 DFT+U 计算，研究了六方交流磁体 CrSb 中的能带分裂。这些研究中发现的费米面的形状、位置甚至对称性各不相同。所开发的方法基于对称性考虑，使我们能够建立交流磁体 CrSb 中能带分裂的几个一般性质，包括每个电子能带中自旋分布的对称性、外部磁场中能带的对称性以及量子振荡的频率和振幅对磁场的依赖性。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.15131v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Altermegnets are a class of metallic magnets characterized by spin-split electron bands. Band splitting in the hexagonal altermagnet CrSb was studied using the ARPES method, magnetotransport and torque measurements, combined with DFT+U calculations. The shape, position, and even symmetry of the Fermi surfaces found in these studies vary. The developed approach, based on symmetry considerations, allows us to establish several general properties of band splitting in the altermagnet CrSb, including the symmetry of the spin distribution in each electron band, the symmetry of the bands in an external magnetic field, and the dependence of the frequencies and amplitudes of quantum oscillations on the magnetic field.

页内定位所在专题
中文摘要

arXiv:2602.15185v1 公告类型：新 摘要：动力系统中存在的“复杂性”的数据驱动表征仍然是一个在物理科学领域广泛应用的开放性问题。我们研究了二维铁磁伊辛模型的“结构复杂性”，这是一个在特定临界温度下表现出二阶相变的范例系统，通常被引用为复杂形态的典型例子。我们通过算法信息论的视角，通过标准无损图像压缩算法近似晶格配置的柯尔莫哥洛夫复杂度，定义了这种结构复杂性的定量度量mathcal Cₛ。我们通过将配置的可压缩性与其按像素排序和随机打乱的对应配置的可压缩性进行比较来规范我们提出的指标 mathcal Cₛ。我们得出 mathcal Cₛ 的定义，作为分别代表系统偏离完美有序和无序的两个分量的乘积，然后将其绘制为温度的函数。我们的数值模拟揭示了已知临界温度 T_c 下 mathcal Cₛ 的明显峰值。这一结果表明，此类信息论测量可以充当敏感的、与模型无关的关键性指标，直接量化有序与混沌之间边界处复杂结构的出现，为无法获得分析解决方案的领域中的数据驱动应用程序打开大门。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.15185v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: The data-driven characterization of the ``complexity'' present in dynamical systems remains an open problem with broad applications across the physical sciences. We investigate the ``structural complexity'' of the 2D ferromagnetic Ising model, a paradigmatic system exhibiting a second-order phase transition at a certain critical temperature which is often cited as a canonical example of complex morphology. We define a quantitative metric for this structural complexity, mathcal Cₛ, through the lens of algorithmic information theory by approximating the Kolmogorov complexity of lattice configurations via standard lossless image compression algorithms. We regularize our proposed metric, mathcal Cₛ, by comparing the compressibility of a configuration to that of its pixel-wise sorted and randomly shuffled counterparts. We arrive at a definition of mathcal Cₛ as a product of two components representing the systems departure from perfect order and disorder respectively which we then plot as a function of temperature. Our numerical simulations reveal a distinct peak in mathcal Cₛ at the known critical temperature T_c. This result demonstrates that such information-theoretic measures can act as sensitive, model-agnostic indicators of criticality, directly quantifying the emergence of complex structure at the boundary between order and chaos, opening the door to data-driven applications in domains where analytic solutions are unavailable.

arXiv:2602.15465v1 公告类型：新 摘要：莫尔半导体提供库仑相互作用和能带拓扑交织在一起的平坦能带，而层间耦合在形成莫尔势方面发挥着核心作用。然而，有限的层间耦合强度和缺乏有效的调谐方法阻碍了对莫尔半导体中相关现象的进一步探索。在这里，我们介绍了一种使用氦气作为压力介质的低温双门金刚石砧平台，可在扭曲双层 WSe2 中实现可逆流体静力学调谐和磁光光谱。压力增强莫尔势，使激子红移，并稳定斯通纳铁磁性，否则在 3.1 度扭曲时不存在。同时，半填充的 C = 1 Chern 绝缘态增强，表现出饱和场减小。此外，我们在 2 GPa 左右观察到从陈绝缘体到莫特绝缘体的拓扑相变。第一性原理计算表明，伽玛到 K 价带最大转换通过将类伊辛拓扑 K 谷微带转换为自旋简并平凡伽玛微带来驱动这种转变。我们的研究结果表明，静水压力是莫尔材料中相关磁性和拓扑带工程的强大、连续的控制轴。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.15465v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Moiré semiconductors offer flat bands where Coulomb interactions and band topology intertwine, while interlayer coupling plays a central role in forming the moiré potential. However, limited interlayer coupling strength and the lack of efficient tuning methods hinder further exploration of correlated phenomena in moiré semiconductors. Here we introduce a cryogenic dual-gated diamond-anvil platform using helium as a pressure medium, enabling reversible hydrostatic tuning together with magneto-optical spectroscopy in twisted bilayer WSe2. Pressure enhances the moiré potential, redshifts excitons, and stabilizes Stoner ferromagnetism otherwise absent at a 3.1-degree twist. Simultaneously, the half-filled C = 1 Chern insulating state strengthens, exhibiting a reduced saturation field. Moreover, we observe a topological phase transition from a Chern insulator to a Mott insulator at around 2 GPa. First-principles calculations reveal that a Gamma-to-K valence-band-maximum switching drives this transition by converting an Ising-like topological K-valley miniband into a spin-degenerate trivial Gamma miniband. Our findings demonstrate hydrostatic pressure as a powerful, continuous control axis for correlated magnetism and topological band engineering in moiré materials.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.15466v1 公告类型：新 摘要：对称性破缺和拓扑序同时不同的强相关电子相之间的连续拓扑相变（TPT）在凝聚态物理中具有重要意义，但很少通过实验实现。我们报告了在角度对齐的 MoTe2/WSe2 莫尔异质双层中半填充 (nu = 1) 时两个连续电场驱动的 TPT。随着面外位移场的增加，几何挫败莫特绝缘体演变成铁磁量子反常霍尔（QAH）莫特绝缘体，即没有可观察到的电荷间隙闭合的自旋极化拓扑莫特绝缘体，随后演变成反铁磁、谷相干莫特绝缘体（VC-AFM），伴随着连续电荷间隙塌缩和临界金属态的出现。层分辨磁圆二色性 (MCD)、磁输运和压缩性测量共同确定相图。反铁磁态的高场演化揭示了临界场 B* 处的类似变磁的转变，在该转变上方再次出现了陈绝缘输运响应。我们的结果将 MoTe2/WSe2 云纹平台建立为扩展 Kane-Mele-Hubbard 模型的可调实现，该模型托管顺序相关拓扑交织的转变。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.15466v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Consecutive topological phase transitions (TPTs) between strongly correlated electronic phases that differ simultaneously in symmetry breaking and topological order are of fundamental interest in condensed matter physics, yet are rarely realized experimentally. We report two consecutive electric-field-driven TPTs at half filling (nu = 1) in angle-aligned MoTe2/WSe2 moire heterobilayers. With increasing out-of-plane displacement field, a geometrically frustrated Mott insulator evolves into a ferromagnetic quantum anomalous Hall (QAH) Mott insulator, i.e., a spin-polarized topological Mott insulator without an observable charge-gap closure, and subsequently into an antiferromagnetic, valley-coherent Mott insulator (VC-AFM) accompanied by a continuous charge-gap collapse and the emergence of a critical metallic state. Layer-resolved magnetic circular dichroism (MCD), magneto-transport, and compressibility measurements jointly determine the phase diagram. The high-field evolution of the antiferromagnetic state reveals a metamagnetic-like transition at a critical field B*, above which a Chern insulating transport response reappears. Our results establish the MoTe2/WSe2 moire platform as a tunable realization of an extended Kane-Mele-Hubbard model hosting sequential correlation-topology-intertwined transitions.

arXiv:2602.15495v1 公告类型：新 摘要：我们研究了随机重置的最近邻 Ising 模型的非平衡动力学，其中系统间歇性地返回到磁化强度 m₀ 的初始配置，重置间时间从幂律分布 α τ₀^α / τα⁺¹ 中得出。重尾重置产生的磁化强度分布与平衡动力学和先前研究的具有指数分布重置时间的伊辛模型显着不同。在二维中，对于 T > T_C，我们找到所有 α 的准铁态，其标记为在 m=0 和 m=m₀ 处发散的双峰分布； α 1 不存在稳态。对于 T α^*。一维和二维的分析结果在模拟的支持下，在 (T,α) 平面上产生了丰富的相图，并揭示了重尾重置如何生成与指数重置情况下看到的非常不同的非平衡相。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.15495v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: We investigate the nonequilibrium dynamics of the nearest-neighbour Ising model subjected to stochastic resetting, where the system is intermittently returned to an initial configuration with magnetisation m₀, with the inter-reset times drawn from the power law distribution α τ₀^α / τα⁺¹. The heavy-tailed resets generate magnetisation distributions that differ significantly from both equilibrium dynamics and the previously studied Ising model with exponentially distributed reset times. In two dimensions, for T > T_C, we find a quasi-ferro state for all α, marked by a double-peaked distribution that diverges at m=0 and m=m₀; no steady state exists for α < 1, while a stationary state emerges for α > 1. For T < T_C, power law resetting produces two distinct regimes separated by a crossover exponent α^* = 1-c: a single-peak ferromagnetic phase localised at mₑq for α < α^*, and a dual-peak ferromagnetic phase with divergences at mₑq and m₀ for α > α^*. Analytic results in one and two dimensions, supported by simulations, yield a rich phase diagram in the (T,α) plane and reveal how heavy-tailed resetting generates nonequilibrium phases very different from those seen in the case of exponential resetting.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.15606v1 公告类型：新 摘要：RuO₂ 的磁性基态仍然存在争议，实验证据表明理想块体材料具有非磁性基态，并表明应变薄膜中存在磁性状态。在这里，我通过映射海森堡哈密顿量，研究了通过 DFT+U 技术稳定的块体 RuO₂ 的（假设）交变磁态的 Néel 温度。 Néel 温度随磁矩单调变化，直至大的 +U 项打开带隙并使 RuO₂ 变成半导体。通过此过程获得的最大 Néel 温度为 408,K (U=3,eV)，对于较小的 U，值要小得多。倒易空间特征值分析揭示了由于亚晶格内反铁磁耦合而导致的自旋模型的螺旋磁基态。这种情况类似于同构 β-MnO₂，它是一个原型螺旋磁体。进一步与以U为可调参数的CrO₂和交变磁MnF₂的计算结果进行比较，支持了自旋模型分析的有效性。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.15606v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: The magnetic groundstate of RuO₂ remains controversial, with experimental evidence for a nonmagnetic groundstate of ideal bulk material and indications of a magnetic state in strained thin films. Here, I investigate the Néel temperature of the (hypothetical) altermagnetic state of bulk RuO₂, stabilized via the DFT+U technique, by mapping on a Heisenberg Hamiltonian. The Néel temperature scales monotonously with the magnetic moment up to the point where a large +U term opens a band gap and turns RuO₂ semiconducting. The maximum Néel temperature obtained by this procedure is 408,K at U=3,eV, and much smaller values for smaller U. A reciprocal-space eigenvalue analysis reveals a helimagnetic groundstate of the spin model due to intra-sublattice antiferromagnetic coupling. This situation resembles the isostructural β-MnO₂, which is a prototype helimagnet. Further comparison with calculations on CrO₂ and altermagnetic MnF₂ taking U as an adjustable parameter supports the validity of the spin model analysis.

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.15760v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: We show how the micro-focused BLS signal of forward volume spin waves is formed and why it remains observable despite symmetry-based "suppression" expectations. A reciprocity-theorem based model with vectorial diffraction-limited focusing identifies the nonnegligible longitudinal focal-field component as the key element responsible for BLS sensitivity in the forward volume geometry. We further demonstrate that full polarization analysis, implemented through polarizer-analyzer maps of coherently excited spin waves, provides information beyond the conventional crossed polarizer-analyzer readout. In a BiYIG thin film, the measured maps exhibit Stokes/anti-Stokes polarization asymmetries and nontrivial patterns that stem from quadratic magneto-optical coupling terms. Fitting the data with a model including Voigt and Cotton-Mouton contributions yields an effective Cotton-Mouton constant and shows that the quadratic response is comparable to the linear Voigt contribution.

arXiv:2602.15774v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: We propose a minimal tight-binding model for the electronic interface layer of the LaAlO₃/SrTiO₃ heterostructure with oxygen vacancies. Both the effects of random on-site potentials and Zeeman-like exchange interactions between correlated carriers and magnetic impurities are taken into account. By applying the combined coherent potential approximation (CPA) and dynamical mean-field theory (DMFT) for a ferromagnetic state, we uncover a disordered Fermi-liquid regime for the majority-spins and a low energy scale which controls the transport of the minority-spin carriers, both induced by the magnetic impurities.

中文摘要

arXiv:2405.20518v2 公告类型：替换 摘要：开放驱动的量子系统定义了非平衡相和相变的强大范式；然而，由于耗散的退相干效应，在这种情况下通常不会出现量子相变。在这封信中，我们考虑了受体耗散（速率 Γ）影响的量子伊辛模型，并表明，尽管相关长度仍然有限（因此没有相变），但它在接近基态量子临界点处形成了明显的峰值。虽然标准技术在这种情况下失败了，但我们开发了一种通用的分析方法，该方法在耗散消失的情况下变得精确（Γ→ 0 但有限的 Γ t）。在技术层面上，我们的方法建立在以前的工作基础上，其中系统的状态由缓慢演化的广义吉布斯系综来描述，该系综在扰动处理耗散的同时解释了哈密顿量的可积性。最后，我们证明了一种普遍性，即哈密顿量的可积性破坏扰动会导致相同的行为。为此，我们首先表明，在局部马尔可夫耗散下，保持伊辛对称性的混沌伊辛哈密顿量的稳态，在 Γ → 0 的限制下，与没有耗散的失超动力学的稳态相同。这种有趣的联系使我们能够利用有关淬灭动力学中量子相变特征的最新发现。

English Abstract

arXiv:2405.20518v2 Announce Type: replace Abstract: Open driven quantum systems have defined a powerful paradigm of nonequilibrium phases and phase transitions; however, quantum phase transitions are generically not expected in this setting due to the decohering effect of dissipation. In this Letter, we consider a quantum Ising model subject to bulk dissipation (at rate Γ) and show that, although the correlation length remains finite (hence no phase transition), it develops a pronounced peak close to the ground-state quantum critical point. While standard techniques fail in this regime, we develop a versatile analytical approach that becomes exact with vanishing dissipation (Γ→ 0 but finite Γ t). On a technical level, our approach builds on previous work where the state of the system is described by a slowly evolving generalized Gibbs ensemble that accounts for the integrability of the Hamiltonian while treating dissipation perturbatively. Finally, we demonstrate a kind of universality in that integrability-breaking perturbations of the Hamiltonian lead to the same behavior. To this end, we first show that the steady state of a chaotic Ising Hamiltonian under local Markovian dissipation that preserves the Ising symmetry, and in the limit Γ → 0, is identical to that of quench dynamics in the absence of dissipation. This intriguing connection then allows us to draw on recent findings about quantum phase transition signatures in quench dynamics.

English Abstract

arXiv:2412.06377v2 Announce Type: replace Abstract: We investigate an interface in the transverse field quantum Ising chain connecting an ordered ferromagnetic phase and a disordered paramagnetic phase that are Kramers-Wannier duals of each other. Unlike prior studies focused on non-invertible defects, this interface exhibits a symmetry that combines Kramers-Wannier transformation with spatial reflection. We demonstrate that, under open boundary conditions, this setup gives rise to a discrete Z₄ symmetry, encompassing the conventional Z₂ Ising parity as a subgroup, while in a closed geometry a non-invertible symmetry emerges. Using the Jordan-Wigner transformation, we map the spin chain onto a solvable quadratic Majorana fermion system. In this formulation, the Z₄ symmetry is realized manifestly as a parity-dependent reflection operation with respect to a Majorana site, in contrast to the conventional reflection which mirrors with respect to the central link of the Majorana chain. Additionally, we construct Majorana strong zero modes that retain the Z₄ symmetry, ensure degeneracies of all energy eigenstates, and are robust under generic local symmetry-preserving perturbations of the fermion model, including interactions. In an open geometry of the studied model, we identify two regimes that exhibit different degeneracy patterns. We discuss whether this is a manifestation of distinct fermion symmetry-protected topological orders protected by the Z₄ symmetry.

arXiv:2507.08072v3 公告类型：替换 摘要：交替磁体构成一类共线磁体，具有动量相关的自旋分裂和消失的净磁化强度。然而，直接观察特征交变自旋分裂仍然具有挑战性。间接特征可以通过传输研究获得，到目前为止，传输研究只考虑了同质驾驶场。我们建议利用不均匀电场和自旋密度梯度通过传输测量来探测交磁费米表面的形状和自旋极化。通过使用半经典玻尔兹曼方法和晶格凯尔迪什形式主义，我们表明交变磁体激发旋转电流和自旋电流，其轮廓取决于交变磁瓣相对于样本边界的相对方向。这些电流可以通过磁力测量技术来测量。与之前考虑输运流体动力学状态的提议不同，即使在欧姆状态下也可以观察到旋流，并且完全依赖于交变磁自旋分裂，而在铁磁体中没有观察到旋流。这里预测的电力和自旋流涡旋在实验上可访问的设置中提供了不同的交变磁签名。

English Abstract

arXiv:2507.08072v3 Announce Type: replace Abstract: Altermagnets constitute a class of collinear magnets with momentum-dependent spin splitting and vanishing net magnetization. Direct observation of the characteristic altermagnetic spin splitting, however, remains challenging. Indirect signatures can be obtained via transport studies, which so far have only considered homogeneous driving fields. We propose to leverage nonuniform electric fields and spin density gradients to probe the shape and the spin polarization of altermagnetic Fermi surfaces via transport measurements. By using both a semiclassical Boltzmann approach and a lattice Keldysh formalism, we show that altermagnets excite swirling electric and spin currents whose profiles depend on the relative orientation of altermagnetic lobes with respect to the sample boundaries. These currents can be measured via magnetometry techniques. Unlike previous proposals considering the hydrodynamic regime of transport, swirling currents are observed even in the Ohmic regime and rely exclusively on the altermagnetic spin splitting, with no swirls observed in ferromagnets. The electric and spin current vortices predicted here provide a different altermagnetic signature in an experimentally accessible setup.

English Abstract

arXiv:2509.12988v4 Announce Type: replace Abstract: We present an SU(2)xU(1) genralization of the Ginzburg-Landau theory for the spin triplet ferromagnetic superconductivity which could also describe the physics of the spin triplet magnon spintronics, where the SU(2) gauge interaction of the magnon plays an important role. The theory is made of the massive photon, massless neutral magnon, massive non-Abelian magnon, and the Higgs scalar field which represents the density of the Copper pair. It has the following characteristic features, the long range magnetic interaction mediated by the massless magnon, two types of conserved supercurrents (the ordinary charge current and the spin current of the magnons), and the non-Abelian Meissner effect generated by the spin current. Moreover, it has non-Abelian topological objects, the quantized non-Abelian magnonic vortex and non-Abelian magnonic monopole, as well as the ordinary Abrikosov vortex. The theory is characterized by three scales. In addition to the correlation length fixed by the mass of the Higgs field it has two different mass scales, the one fixed by the mass of the photon and the other fixed by the mass of the off-diagonal magnon. We compare the theory with the non-Abelian gauge theory of the spin doublet ferromagnetic superconductivity which could also be interpreted as an effective theory of the electron spintronics. We discuss the physical implications of the non-Abelian gauge theories in condensed matter physics.

English Abstract

arXiv:2510.11350v2 Announce Type: replace Abstract: Magnetic materials are crucial for manipulating electron spin and magnetic fields, enabling applications in data storage, spintronics, charge transport, and energy conversion, while also providing insight into fundamental quantum phenomena. In numerous applications, the interaction between electrons and lattice vibrations, known as electron-phonon coupling, can be of significant importance. In that regard, we extend the EPW package to be able to interpolate the electron-phonon matrix elements combining perturbation theory and maximally localized Wannier functions. This allows to use dense momentum grids at a reasonable computational cost when computing electron-phonon-related quantities and physical properties. We validate our implementation considering ferromagnetic iron and nickel, where we explore the absence of phonon-driven superconductivity, finding that superconductivity is intrinsically suppressed. Furthermore, we evaluate the carrier resistivity at finite temperatures for both systems, considering the role of the magnetic phase in carrier transport. Our findings indicate that in the case of Fe, the primary contributor to resistivity is electron-phonon scattering. In contrast, for Ni, electron-phonon scattering constitutes less than one-third of the resistivity, underscoring a fundamental difference in the transport properties of the two systems.

arXiv:2510.14868v3 公告类型：替换 摘要：交变磁体 (AM) - 具有自旋分裂能带结构且净自旋极化为零的磁性材料，可根据哈密顿量中交变磁项的强度分为弱或强。我们从理论上研究强交变磁相和弱交变磁相下两个 AM 之间连接处的电子传输。电荷和自旋电导率被分析为两个 AM 的 N'eel 矢量之间的角度 θ 的函数。在强 AM 状态下，电荷电导率随着 θ → π 的变化而消失，而在弱 AM 状态下，电荷电导率仍然有限。在两个 AM 之间引入普通金属 (NM) 会导致电荷电导率发生法布里-P 型振荡，该振荡可以通过施加的栅极电压进行控制。在强状态下，AM-NM-AM 结中的传输由上自旋电子主导，而两个自旋通道在弱状态下都有贡献。这些结果凸显了基于AM的异质结构在自旋电子应用中的潜力，例如自旋滤波器和基于量子干涉的自旋电子器件，其中可调谐的自旋相关输运和干涉效应可以在电子器件中利用，而无需外部施加磁场。

English Abstract

arXiv:2510.14868v3 Announce Type: replace Abstract: Altermagnets (AMs) - magnetic materials that have spin-split bandstructure with zero net spin polarization can be classified as weak or strong depending upon the strength of altermagnetic term in the Hamiltonian. We theoretically investigate electron transport in junctions between the two AMs in strong and weak altermagnetic phases. The charge and spin conductivities are analyzed as functions of angle θ between the Néel vectors of the two AMs. In the strong AM regime, the charge conductivity vanishes as θ → π, while in the weak AM regime it remains finite. Introducing a normal metal (NM) between two AMs leads to Fabry-Pérot-type oscillations in charge conductivity which can be controlled by an applied gate voltage. In the strong regime, transport in AM-NM-AM junctions is dominated by up-spin electrons, whereas both spin channels contribute in the weak regime. These results highlight the potential of AM-based heterostructures for spintronic applications, such as spin filters, and quantum interference-based spintronic devices, where tunable spin-dependent transport and interference effects can be utilized in electronic devices without a need for externally applied magnetic field.

中文摘要

arXiv:2511.08426v2 公告类型：替换 摘要：磁各向异性对于维持二维材料 (2D) 中的长程磁序至关重要，任何计算临界温度的近似方案都必须考虑到磁各向异性。虽然二维铁磁体在预测居里温度方面受到了极大的关注，但二维反铁磁性的处理在很大程度上仅限于经典方法，这些方法通常会低估镍原子温度。反铁磁性的概念可以被视为单Q磁序的特例，对于此类系统，可以使用荷斯坦-普里马科夫（HP）玻色子化或基于格林函数的随机相位近似（RPA）从磁振子色散计算临界温度。在这里，我们研究了 HP 和 RPA 方法中单离子各向异性对一般单 Q 系统的影响。就 RPA 而言，我们概括了该方法，包括卡伦去耦 (CD) 校正，该校正先前已被证明与二维铁磁体的实验居里温度具有良好的一致性。我们将 CrI₃（单轴铁磁体）、MPS₃（M=Ni, Mn, Fe）（单轴反铁磁体）和 CrSBr（三轴铁磁体）单层的计算临界温度与实验值进行比较，发现基于 Green 函数的方法比 HP 更可靠，并且如果单离子各向异性很大，CD 去耦似乎比 RPA 更准确。

English Abstract

arXiv:2511.08426v2 Announce Type: replace Abstract: Magnetic anisotropy is crucial for sustaining long range magnetic order in two-dimensional materials (2D) and must be taken into account by any approximate scheme for calculating critical temperatures. While 2D ferromagnets have received significant attention with regard to predicting Curie temperatures, the treatment of 2D anti-ferromagnetism has largely been restricted to classical approaches, which typically underestimate Néel temperatures. The concept of anti-ferromagnetism can be regarded as a special case of single-Q magnetic order, and for such systems the critical temperature can be calculated from the magnon dispersion using either Holstein-Primakoff (HP) bosonization or Green's function-based Random Phase Approximation (RPA). Here, we study the effects of single-ion anisotropy in general single-Q systems in both the HP and RPA methods. In the case of RPA, we generalize the approach to include the Callen Decoupling (CD) correction, which has previously been shown to yield good agreement with experimental Curie temperatures for 2D ferromagnets. We compare the calculated critical temperatures of CrI₃ (uniaxial ferromagnet), MPS₃ (M=Ni, Mn, Fe) (uniaxial anti-ferromagnets) and CrSBr (triaxial ferromagnet) monolayers with experimental values and find that the Green's function-based methods are much more reliable than HP and that the CD decoupling appears to be more accurate than RPA if the single-ion anisotropy is large.

arXiv:2511.10503v2 发布类型：替换 摘要：多种材料可以通过自旋 1/2 海森堡梯子近似描述。在这里，密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）算法与先前建立的数值自洽平均场近似一起用于研究第二维耦合的自旋梯的磁性。包括自旋间隙、反铁磁、亚铁磁和全极化相的全基态相图被呈现为梯间和梯内耦合以及磁场的函数。通过测量磁化强度对所施加磁场的依赖性，可以在相图上定位材料并确定哈密顿参数。这些结果为识别和表征由耦合自旋梯组成的磁性材料提供了一条实用途径。

English Abstract

arXiv:2511.10503v2 Announce Type: replace Abstract: A large variety of materials can be approximately described by means of spin-1/2 Heisenberg ladders. Here, the Density Matrix Renormalization Group (DMRG) algorithm together with a previously established numerical self-consistent mean-field approximation is used to investigate the magnetic properties of spin ladders coupled in a second dimension. The full ground state phase diagram including spin-gapped, antiferromagnetic, ferrimagnetic and fully polarized phases is presented as a function of interladder and intraladder coupling and magnetic field. Measurement of the dependence of magnetization on applied magnetic field is shown to enable location of a material on the phase diagram and determination of the Hamiltonian parameters. These results provide a practical route toward identifying and characterizing magnetic materials composed of coupled spin ladders.

English Abstract

arXiv:2506.20366v4 Announce Type: replace-cross Abstract: Ultrafast pump-probe imaging reveals that the efficiency of optical excitation of coherent spins waves in epitaxial iron garnet films can be effectively controlled by an external electric field at room temperature. 中文摘要

arXiv:2602.13341v1 公告类型：新 摘要：纳米级磁性层中的超顺磁性是各种基于自旋电子的传感器和计算应用的关键特性。虽然传统的磁化测量可以检测超顺磁特征，但它们通常需要应用高扰动场，并且对于集成在功能设备内的磁性层来说很难实现。在这项研究中，我们通过使用基于氮空位 (NV) 中心的量子相移测量法探测其低频近场电磁 (EM) 波动，非侵入性地研究了沉积在金刚石基板上的厚度为 1.1 nm 的纳米级 CoFeB 层的超顺磁自旋动力学。我们的测量揭示了 NV 中心相移时间的非常规、非单调温度依赖性，我们将其归因于 CoFeB 中热驱动的超顺磁畴翻转产生的电磁波动。我们的研究结果得到了 NV 中心失相动力学的理论解释和 CoFeB 层基于 SQUID 的互补磁化特性的进一步支持。此外，利用 NV 相移技术，我们提取了 CoFeB 中电磁波动的谱密度，用于隔离作用于 NV 中心的电磁波动的不同分量。我们还测量了 NV 中心的 CoFeB 到 NV 距离相关的相干时间，以研究 CoFeB 层的维数对生成的近场电磁波动的影响。这些结果为纳米级磁性层的磁化动力学和近场电磁环境提供了重要的见解。它还对混合量子自旋电子器件的开发和涉及纳米级光磁材料的应用具有重大影响。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.13341v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Superparamagnetism in nanoscale magnetic layers is a critical property for a wide range of spintronic-based sensor and computing applications. While conventional magnetization measurements can detect superparamagnetic signatures, they often require the application of high perturbative fields and are difficult to implement for magnetic layers integrated within functional devices. In this study, we non-invasively investigate the superparamagnetic spin dynamics of a nanoscale CoFeB layer of thickness 1.1 nm, deposited on a diamond substrate, by probing its low-frequency near-field electromagnetic (EM) fluctuations using nitrogen-vacancy (NV) centers-based quantum dephasometry. Our measurements reveal an unconventional, non-monotonic temperature dependence of the dephasing time of NV centers, which we attribute to EM fluctuations produced by thermally driven superparamagnetic domain flipping in CoFeB. Our findings are further supported by the theoretical interpretation of the dephasing dynamics of NV centers and the complementary SQUID-based magnetization characterizations of the CoFeB layer. Additionally, exploiting the technique of NV dephasometry, we extract the spectral density of the EM fluctuations in CoFeB, which is used to isolate different components of the EM fluctuations acting on NV centers. We also measure the CoFeB-to-NV distance-dependent coherence times of NV centers to investigate the effect of the dimensionality of the CoFeB layer on the generated near-field EM fluctuations. These results provide critical insight into the magnetization dynamics and near-field EM environment of nanoscale magnetic layers. It also has significant implications for the development of hybrid quantum spintronic devices and applications involving nanoscale opto-magnetic materials.

页内定位所在专题
中文摘要

arXiv:2602.13390v1 公告类型：新 摘要：亚稳态，即在真正的渐近平衡出现之前部分弛豫到长期存在的准稳态，由于时间尺度分离而普遍出现在经典和量子动力系统中。在开放量子系统中，本质上非平衡的类似物，即动态亚稳态，可以源自非厄米算子的谱几何。在非交互模型中，这种机制会产生边界敏感的异常松弛、瞬态放大和拓扑规定的长寿命边缘模式，所有这些都会随着系统规模的增长而增强。在这里，我们将动态亚稳态扩展到非线性、相互作用的领域，并将磁性异质结构确定为其探索的自然平台。我们引入了一种相互作用的自旋 Lindbladian，其线性化磁振子动力学映射到动态亚稳态 Hatano-Nelson 链上，并表明非相互作用极限中的动态亚稳定性产生了真正的非线性现象，包括尺寸相关的自旋下降和对不稳定平衡的异常吸引。与拓扑规定的狄拉克玻色子相关的长寿命边缘态在非线性和无序状态下持续存在。我们进一步分析了经典 Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert-Slonczewski 框架内磁性多层膜的磁化动力学，将 Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya 相互作用、非局域阻尼和自旋转移扭矩确定为控制体边界稳定性失配和能带拓扑的控制参数。虽然之前确定的所有独特的动力学现象都在这个实验相关的环境中重新出现，但 LLGS 框架还支持量子模型中不存在的多稳定性和极限环。我们的结果构成了非线性动力学中动态亚稳态的第一个系统研究，与自旋力矩振荡器阵列、磁振子器件等直接相关。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.13390v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Metastability, i.e., partial relaxation to long-lived, quasi-stationary states before true asymptotic equilibrium sets in, emerges ubiquitously in classical and quantum dynamical systems as a result of timescales separation. In open quantum systems, an intrinsically nonequilibrium analogue, dynamical metastability, can originate from the spectral geometry of a non-Hermitian operator. In noninteracting models, this mechanism produces boundary-sensitive anomalous relaxation, transient amplification, and topologically mandated long-lived edge modes, all of which are enhanced as system size grows. Here we extend dynamical metastability into the nonlinear, interacting regime and identify magnetic heterostructures as a natural platform for its exploration. We introduce an interacting spin Lindbladian whose linearized magnon dynamics map onto a dynamically metastable Hatano-Nelson chain, and show that dynamical metastability in the noninteracting limit seeds genuinely nonlinear phenomena, including size-dependent spin dipping and anomalous attraction to unstable equilibria. Long-lived edge states associated to topologically mandated Dirac bosons persist under nonlinearities and disorder. We further analyze the magnetization dynamics in magnetic multilayers within the classical Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert-Slonczewski framework, identifying Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction, nonlocal damping, and spin-transfer torque as control parameters governing bulk-boundary stability mismatch and band topology. While all the distinctive dynamical phenomena previously identified reappear in this experimentally relevant setting, the LLGS framework also supports multistability and limit cycles that are absent in the quantum model. Our results constitute the first systematic study of dynamical metastability in nonlinear dynamics, directly relevant to spin-torque oscillator arrays, magnonic devices, and beyond.

三聚体钌酸盐 Ba4Ru3O10 的隐藏密度波不稳定性#

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.13443v1 公告类型：新 摘要：我们报告了基于三聚体的钌酸盐 Ba4Ru3O10 中隐藏的密度波不稳定性，该材料之前被认为是纯反铁磁体，在 TA=100 K 处具有相变。这种转变体现在晶格参数、输运、热力学和磁化率中，但对高达至少 14 T 的磁场仍然非常不敏感，表明电子驱动重建。在低得多的温度 T*= 20 K 下，电荷传输变得强烈非线性，表现出明显的脱钉阈值、负微分电阻、明显的电流和频率依赖性以及赫兹范围内的缓慢集体动态。虽然每个特征都是密度波传输的特征，但它们同时出现在反铁磁氧化物中是前所未有的。所有非线性特征仅在 3% Ir 替代后消失，这保留了晶体结构和绝缘状态，排除了焦耳热或外在伪影。 TA 处的电子重构与 T* 处非线性动力学的出现之间的广泛分离表明 Ba4Ru3O10 是一种罕见的相关系统，具有与反铁磁性交织在一起的强固定集体电子态。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.13443v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: We report a hidden density-wave instability in the trimer-based ruthenate Ba4Ru3O10, previously regarded as a pure antiferromagnet with a phase transition at TA=100 K. This transition is manifested in lattice parameters, transport, thermodynamics, and magnetic susceptibility, yet remains remarkably insensitive to magnetic fields up to at least 14 T, indicating an electronically driven reconstruction. At much lower temperatures T*= 20 K, charge transport becomes strongly nonlinear, exhibiting distinct depinning thresholds, negative differential resistance, pronounced current- and frequency-dependence, and slow collective dynamics in the Hertz range. While each feature is characteristic of density-wave transport, their simultaneous occurrence in an antiferromagnetic oxide is unprecedented. All nonlinear signatures vanish upon only 3% Ir substitution, which preserves the crystal structure and insulating state, ruling out Joule heating or extrinsic artifacts. The wide separation between the electronic reconstruction at TA and the emergence of nonlinear dynamics at T* identifies Ba4Ru3O10 as a rare correlated system hosting a strongly pinned collective electronic state intertwined with antiferromagnetism.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.13590v1 公告类型：新 摘要：交变磁力源自复合实空间和自旋空间对称性，将零净磁化强度与明显的动量相关自旋分裂相结合。本综述强调了角分辨光电子能谱 (ARPES) 及其自旋分辨 (SARPES) 和圆二色性 (CD-ARPES) 变体在直接可视化交变磁体中的非相对论能带分裂和自旋纹理方面的关键作用。在自旋群框架内，我们区分了铁磁、反铁磁和交磁序，并阐明了自旋极化的对称起源。然后，我们系统地回顾了代表性系统：有争议的 d 波原型 RuO2、层状 d 波交替磁体 KV2Se2O 和 Rb1-delta V2Te2O、一系列 g 波化合物，包括 MnTe（域可调）和 CrSb（拓扑），以及非共面反铁磁体 MnTe2 和其他新兴候选平台。总体而言，ARPES 已成为解决对称驱动的自旋分裂的关键探针。微/纳米束和原位光谱学的未来进展，结合应变和域工程、异质结构设计以及更广泛的非常规磁态的探索，预计将推动交变磁学和光电子能谱的共同发展，为自旋电子学和相关量子研究铺平道路。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.13590v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Altermagnetism arises from composite real-space and spin-space symmetries, combining zero net magnetization with pronounced momentum-dependent spin splitting. This review highlights the pivotal role of angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (ARPES), along with its spin-resolved (SARPES) and circular-dichroism (CD-ARPES) variants, in directly visualizing nonrelativistic band splitting and spin textures in altermagnets. Within the spin-group framework, we distinguish ferromagnetic, antiferromagnetic, and altermagnetic orders and elucidate the symmetry origin of spin polarization. We then systematically review representative systems: the debated d-wave prototype RuO2, layered d-wave altermagnets KV2Se2O and Rb1-delta V2Te2O, and a series of g-wave compounds including MnTe (domain-tunable) and CrSb (topological), together with the noncoplanar antiferromagnet MnTe2 and other emerging candidate platforms. Overall, ARPES has become a key probe for resolving symmetry-driven spin splitting. Future advances in micro/nano-beam and in-situ spectroscopies, combined with strain and domain engineering, heterostructure design, and exploration of broader unconventional magnetic states, are expected to drive the joint evolution of altermagnetism and photoemission spectroscopy, paving the way for spintronic and correlated quantum research.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.13593v1 公告类型：新 摘要：我们从理论上提出并分析了类约瑟夫森磁隧道结（MTJ）结构，该结构表现出类似于超导约瑟夫森结中的量子自旋动力学。通过利用具有易平面各向异性的低耗散 MTJ 运动方程与约瑟夫森相动力学之间的同构，我们构建了实现自旋电子量子位的理论框架。在这个框架内，我们确定了控制从经典行为到量子行为转变的物理参数，例如各向异性常数、吉尔伯特阻尼、自旋电流幅度和几何因素。我们证明了不同类型的自旋电子量子位，包括电荷、通量和传输超导量子位的类似物，可以根据能量尺度的层次结构来实现。为每个状态开发了哈密顿形式主义，从而能够对两级量子动力学进行分析处理并估计相干时间。特别是，我们证明自旋电流不仅可以用于激发，还可以通过耗散控制来稳定量子位状态。这些发现提供了一条将自旋电子量子位集成到 CMOS 兼容架构中的途径，并为用于量子计算的完全自旋电子平台奠定了基础。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.13593v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: We theoretically propose and analyze a Josephson-like magnetic tunnel junction (MTJ) structure that exhibits quantum spin dynamics analogous to those in superconducting Josephson junctions. By exploiting the isomorphism between the equations of motion for low-dissipation MTJs with easy-plane anisotropy and the Josephson phase dynamics, we construct a theoretical framework for realizing spintronic qubits. Within this framework, we identify the physical parameters -- such as anisotropy constants, Gilbert damping, spin current amplitude, and geometric factors -- that govern the transition from classical to quantum behavior. We show that different types of spintronic qubits, including analogs of charge, flux, and transmon superconducting qubits, can be implemented depending on the hierarchy of energy scales. A Hamiltonian formalism is developed for each regime, enabling an analytical treatment of the two-level quantum dynamics and estimation of coherence times. In particular, we demonstrate that the spin current can be used not only to excite but also to stabilize the qubit states through dissipation control. These findings provide a route toward integrating spintronic qubits into CMOS-compatible architectures and lay the groundwork for a fully spintronic platform for quantum computation.

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.13608v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Spontaneous dynamic systems have attracted significant attention for their rich underlying physics such as phase-locking and synchronization. In this work, we report a new mechanism of generating magnetic spontaneous oscillation via parametric pumping. By applying a pump tone to excite propagating spin waves in a yttrium iron garnet delay line, four-wave mixing converts the pump mode into two phase-autonomous propagating magnon modes, i.e. a spontaneous mode with nearly twice the wavenumber of the pump mode and an idler mode with nearly zero wavenumber. This allows us to reliably generate ultrasharp spin wave dynamics with broad frequency tunability from the pump and magnetic field. We show that the spontaneous mode can be phase-locked to a probe tone, similar to an auto-oscillator. Furthermore, the spontaneous dynamics can be used to implement a high-gain magnonic parametric amplifier with a gain up to 40 dB. Our results open a new avenue for studying nonlinear magnonics and synchronization physics in propagating magnon geometry and for developing new magnonic devices.

arXiv:2602.13643v1 公告类型：新 摘要：具有交替自旋分裂的强关联电子系统中磁关联的演化在很大程度上仍未得到探索。在这里，我们研究自旋相关的次近邻跳跃 t' 产生的自旋分裂如何重塑二维方格哈伯德模型中的费米表面嵌套和范霍夫奇点，从而导致磁不稳定性的演化。使用约束路径量子蒙特卡罗方法，我们通过计算动量分辨的自旋结构因子找到了作为填充函数和 t'/t 的主要磁相关性。分析揭示了在增加自旋相关各向异性或掺杂远离半填充时，各向同性半填充系统中的反铁磁 (π,π) 阶到非共线螺旋 (π,q) 阶的转变，最终进入条纹和螺旋相关共存的短程相关状态。这些发现强调了在交流磁系统中实现螺旋相关性的可能途径，可能为利用非共线自旋纹理的自旋电子器件提供一个平台。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.13643v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: The evolution of magnetic correlation in strongly correlated electron systems with altermagentic spin splitting remains largely unexplored. Here we investigate how spin splitting generated by spin-dependent next-nearest-neighbor hopping t' reshapes the Fermi surface nesting and van Hove singularities in the two-dimensional square-lattice Hubbard model, leading evolution of magnetic instabilities. Using the constrained-path quantum Monte Carlo method, we find the dominant magnetic correlation as functions of the filling and t'/t by computing the momentum-resolved spin structure factor. The analysis reveals a transition from antiferromagnetic (π,π) order in the isotropic, half-filled system to non-collinear spiral (π,q) order upon increasing the spin-dependent anisotropy or doping away from half-filling, ultimately entering a short-range correlation regime where stripe and spiral correlation coexist. These findings highlight a possible route to realizing spiral correlation in altermagnetic systems, potentially providing a platform for spintronic devices that exploit non-collinear spin textures.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.13709v1 公告类型：新 摘要：耦合到陈绝缘体的局部磁矩的强方向无序会产生无法连续连接到干净极限的拓扑相，因此是真正的无序驱动。我们在二维陈绝缘体的自旋 Qi-Wu-Zhang 模型中证明了这一点，该模型与单位长度的无序经典自旋耦合。使用两种互补的方法对拓扑相图进行数值计算：扭曲边界条件和拓扑哈密顿技术。我们的结果表明，强无序可以作为一种基本的拓扑机制，而不仅仅是一种扰动。对于强交换耦合，调整质量参数揭示了具有不同陈数 C 的相之间的转变。值得注意的是，这种转变是由跨越化学势的无序平均格林函数的零点而不是极点驱动的，并且在任何清洁系统中都没有类似物。我们进一步确定了一个 C = 0 的强耦合相，尽管如此，它在拓扑上并不平凡，其特征是在经典自旋配置流形上有一个独特的陈数 C⁽S⁾ ≠ 0。这个阶段也是无序驱动的，因为 C⁽S⁾ = 0 在干净的极限中。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.13709v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Strong directional disorder in local magnetic moments coupled to a Chern insulator gives rise to topological phases that cannot be continuously connected to the clean limit and are therefore genuinely disorder-driven. We demonstrate this in a spinful Qi-Wu-Zhang model of a two-dimensional Chern insulator coupled to disordered classical spins of unit length. The topological phase diagram is computed numerically using two complementary approaches: twisted boundary conditions and the topological Hamiltonian technique. Our results show that strong disorder can act as a fundamental topological mechanism rather than merely a perturbation. For strong exchange coupling, tuning the mass parameter reveals a transition between phases with different Chern numbers C. Remarkably, this transition is driven by zeros, rather than poles, of the disorder-averaged Green's function crossing the chemical potential, and has no analogue in any clean system. We further identify a strong-coupling phase with C = 0 that is nonetheless topologically nontrivial, characterized by a distinct Chern number C⁽S⁾ ≠ 0 over the manifold of classical spin configurations. This phase is also disorder-driven, as C⁽S⁾ = 0 in the clean limit.

Polar unidirectional magnetotransport in p-type tellurene from quantum geometry

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.13721v1 公告类型：新 摘要：单向磁阻或电磁手性各向异性 (eMChA) 是一种在非中心对称导体中出现的非线性磁输运现象，其中电阻 R(B) 的变化为： (i) 手性，Δ R(B)/R(0)=2,ḩi, bf Iḑotbf B，或 (ii) 极坐标，Δ R(B)/R(0)=2,γ，bf Iḑot(bf P×bf B)，eMChA 系数为 ḩi 和 γ。在[物理。莱特牧师。 135, 106602 (2025)]，我们证明碲烯导带中的 eMChA 是极性的 (ḩi=0, γ≠ 0)，并且由于其 Weyl 节点而从量子度量偶极子和孤对极化 bf P 中出现。在这里，我们将工作扩展到碲烯的价带，其中 eMChA 通常被认为是手性的 (ḩi ≠ 0, γ = 0)。我们还表明，极性系数 γ ≠ 0 通过下折叠过程自然出现，其中包含能带的远程 Weyl 节点在低能级引起量子度量的动量空间梯度，激活有限度量偶极子。将半经典玻尔兹曼输运与碲烯的 bf kḑotbf p 描述相结合，我们的数值计算与垂直场中纵向电压 V²ømegaₚₐᵣₐₗₗₑₗ₍μ) 的掺杂 (μ) 相关二次谐波测量定量一致。碲烯中 eMChA 的组合手性和极性特征 (ḩi≠0, γ≠ 0) 也解释了平面场中 V²ømegaₚₐᵣₐₗₗₑₗ₍φ) 的角度 (φ) 依赖性的变化。我们的结果表明，极性 eMChA 可以通过多带效应在拓扑平凡能带中出现，并将碲烯建立为电子和空穴体系中量子几何校正的平台。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.13721v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Unidirectional magnetoresistance, or electric magnetochiral anisotropy (eMChA), is a nonlinear magnetotransport phenomenon that arises in noncentrosymmetric conductors , where changes in resistance R(B) are: (i) chiral, Δ R(B)/R(0)=2,ḩi, bf Iḑotbf B, or (ii) polar, Δ R(B)/R(0)=2,γ, bf Iḑot(bf P×bf B), with eMChA coefficients ḩi and γ. In [Phys. Rev. Lett. 135, 106602 (2025)], we showed that the eMChA in the conduction band of tellurene is polar (ḩi=0, γ≠ 0) and emerges from the quantum metric dipole due to its Weyl node and from the lone pair polarization bf P. Here, we extend our work to the valence band of tellurene, where the eMChA is usually said to be chiral (ḩi ≠ 0, γ = 0). We show that also a polar coefficient γ ≠ 0 emerges naturally through a downfolding procedure, in which remote Weyl-node containing bands induce momentum-space gradients of the quantum metric in the low-energy levels, activating finite metric dipoles. Combining semiclassical Boltzmann transport with a bf kḑotbf p description of tellurene, our numerical calculations agree quantitatively with doping (μ) dependent second-harmonic measurements of the longitudinal voltage V²ømegaₚₐᵣₐₗₗₑₗ₍μ) in perpendicular field. The combined chiral and polar characters (ḩi≠0, γ≠ 0) of the eMChA in tellurene also explains the shift in the angular (φ) dependence of V²ømegaₚₐᵣₐₗₗₑₗ₍φ) for in plane fields. Our results demonstrate that the polar eMChA can arise in topologically trivial bands through multiband effects and establishes tellurene as a platform for quantum-geometric rectification in both electron and hole regimes.

页内定位所在专题
中文摘要

arXiv:2602.13768v1 公告类型：新 摘要：相对论自旋动量锁定已在非相对论极限中净磁化强度为零的时间反转破坏类材料中得到证明，例如交流磁体和其他非共线磁体。使用密度泛函理论计算，我们的目标是展示铁磁体中的相对论自旋动量锁定，重点关注具有通过旋转对称连接的磁性位点的一大类铁磁材料，并与面心立方镍进行比较。在SrRuO3中，反对称交换相互作用产生与易轴正交的自旋倾斜，而在所有其他情况下，自旋倾斜是被禁止的。即使真实空间中的倾斜磁矩被禁止，相对论自旋动量锁定在 k 空间中也显示出相当大的贡献。使用原型铁磁体，例如具有 NiAs 晶体结构的正交 SrRuO3、六方 CrTe 和 CrAs、半 Heusler MnPtSb 和 fcc Ni，我们证明相对论自旋动量锁定可以在铁磁体中产生强大的效应。具有通过旋转对称连接的磁性位点的中心对称铁磁材料的次主要成分具有类似于交流磁体的自旋动量锁定，而非中心对称的 MnPtSb 由于自旋轨道耦合而具有相对论性 p 波。 Fcc Ni 表现出更复杂的行为，结合了交流磁体的两种自旋动量锁定模式特征。由于铁磁体通常比交流磁体具有更大的带宽，因此它们为观察偶波相对论自旋动量锁定和相关的新兴现象提供了一个有前景的平台。从应用的角度来看，相对论自旋动量锁定控制着对称允许的自旋霍尔电流、自旋光电流和 k 空间中其他动量相关的自旋响应。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.13768v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: The relativistic spin-momentum locking has been proven in time-reversal-breaking classes of materials with zero net magnetization in the non-relativistic limit, such as altermagnets and other non-collinear magnets. Using density functional theory calculations, we aim to show relativistic spin-momentum locking in ferromagnets, focusing on a broad class of ferromagnetic materials with magnetic sites connected by rotational symmetry, and compare with fcc Ni. In SrRuO3, the antisymmetric exchange interaction produces a spin canting orthogonal to the easy axis, while in all other cases, spin canting is forbidden. Even when the canted magnetic moment in real space is forbidden, relativistic spin-momentum locking shows sizable contributions in k-space. Using prototypical ferromagnets such as orthorhombic SrRuO3, hexagonal CrTe and CrAs with the NiAs crystal structure, half-Heusler MnPtSb, and fcc Ni, we demonstrate that relativistic spin-momentum locking can generate strong effects in ferromagnets. Subdominant components of centrosymmetric ferro-magnetic materials with magnetic sites connected by rotational symmetry host spin-momentum locking similar to altermagnets, while noncentrosymmetric MnPtSb hosts relativistic p-wave due to the spin-orbit coupling. Fcc Ni shows a more complex behavior with a combination of two spin-momentum locking patterns characteristic of altermagnets. Because ferromagnets typically have larger bandwidths than altermagnets, they provide a promising platform for observing even-wave relativistic spin-momentum locking and associated emergent phenomena. From an application standpoint, relativistic spin-momentum locking governs symmetry-allowed spin Hall currents, spin photocurrents, and other momentum-dependent spin responses in k-space.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.13785v1 公告类型：新 摘要：我们全面研究了 Fe 掺杂对插层范德华反铁磁体 Co1-xFexNb3S6（x = 0.1 和 0.3）的晶格动力学、磁有序性和磁输运特性的影响。温度和偏振相关的拉曼散射测量表明，随着 Fe 浓度的增加，180 cm-1 声子模式出现明显的蓝移，表明晶格振动对 Fe 引起的结构和质量效应的敏感性增强。虽然声子模式的温度演化主要由传统的非简声声子软化主导，但在 x = 0.1 的 N'eel 温度附近观察到的细微异常表明弱自旋声子耦合。电传输和磁化率数据显示了反铁磁相变的清晰特征，当 x = 0.1 时，TN ~ 20.5-23.7 K；当 x = 0.3 时，TN ~ 32.0 K。面外磁化强度测量揭示了 x = 0.1 时两个场感应转变的磁滞行为，在 x = 0.3 时演变成单个磁滞回线，表明磁基态的微妙重建。 x = 0.1 时的磁输运测量进一步显示了蝴蝶形磁滞磁阻和弱拓扑霍尔效应；然而，这两个特征在 x = 0.3 时都受到强烈抑制。这些结果说明了铁诱导的磁结构重建在插层范德华反铁磁体的拓扑和磁输运现象微调中的关键作用。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.13785v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: We present a comprehensive investigation of the effects of Fe doping on the lattice dynamics, magnetic ordering, and magneto-transport properties of the intercalated van der Waals antiferromagnets Co1-xFexNb3S6 (x = 0.1 and 0.3). Temperature- and polarization-dependent Raman scattering measurements reveal a pronounced blue shift of the 180 cm-1 phonon mode with increasing Fe concentration, indicating enhanced sensitivity of lattice vibrations to Fe-induced structural and mass effects. While the temperature evolution of the phonon modes is dominated by conventional anharmonic phonon softening, subtle anomalies observed near the Néel temperature for x = 0.1 point to weak spin-phonon coupling. Electrical transport and magnetic susceptibility data show clear signatures of the antiferromagnetic phase transitions at TN ~ 20.5-23.7 K for x = 0.1 and TN ~ 32.0 K for x = 0.3. Out-of-plane magnetization measurements reveal hysteretic behavior with two field-induced transitions for x =0.1, which evolve into a single hysteresis loop at x =0.3, signaling a subtle reconstruction of the magnetic ground state. Magneto-transport measurements for x = 0.1 further display a butterfly-shaped hysteretic magnetoresistance and a weak topological Hall effect; however, both features are strongly suppressed at x = 0.3. These results illustrate the critical role of Fe-induced magnetic structure reconstruction in fine-tuning topological and magnetic transport phenomena in intercalated van der Waals antiferromagnets.

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.13924v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Antiferromagnets typically host spin-wave (magnon) excitations in the terahertz (THz) regime, offering a promising platform for high-speed magnonic information technologies. Harnessing these excitations requires sensitive control of their spectral properties. Here we use resonant x-ray diffraction and Raman scattering to demonstrate uniaxial-strain control of the antiferromagnetic (AFM) ground state and THz magnon excitations in the layered Mott insulator Ca₂RuO₄. Although the states separated by the strain-induced phase transition differ only by the sign of the weak and partially frustrated interlayer interaction, their magnon energies differ by more than 10% (~ 0.3 THz). Our theoretical analysis explains this surprising observation by tracing the origin of both the sign reversal of the interlayer coupling and the magnon energy to the spin-orbital composition of the Ru valence electrons. The extreme strain sensitivity of the THz magnon energy near a magnetic phase transition opens up pathways towards a new generation of transition-edge magnonic devices.

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.13959v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Polycrystalline hafnia-based thin films exhibit mixed ferroelectric (FE), antiferroelectric (AFE), and dielectric (DE) behavior, with switching characteristics strongly influenced by microstructure and phase distribution. Here, we develop a unified grain-resolved three-dimensional phase-field framework for metal-insulator-metal capacitors that simultaneously captures ferroic phase characteristics in realistic polycrystalline microstructures by explicitly incorporating grain topology and crystallographic orientation. Antipolar sublattice kinetics are represented via the coupled evolution of macroscopic and staggered polarization order parameters. All thermodynamic and kinetic parameters are calibrated to experimental P-E hysteresis loops and held fixed across all simulations. The results show that phase fractions primarily determine hysteresis character, while vertical segregation of AFE- and FE-rich regions systematically reduces the effective coercive field (Ec) under identical electrical loading. Grain-resolved analysis reveals that this reduction arises from microstructure-assisted switching pathways and electrostatic coupling between layers. These findings demonstrate that vertical phase arrangement provides a viable strategy to engineer switching behavior in hafnia-based ferroic capacitors and highlight the importance of explicit microstructural resolution for quantitative phase-field modeling.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.14031v1 公告类型：新 摘要：我们展示了一种非易失性磁电磁能存储器 (MEMM)，它可以通过绝缘反铁磁体中的直接磁振子驱动传感实现完全电气写入/读取。制造的 SrIrO3/La-BiFeO3/SrIrO3 三层表现出低于 100 ps 的开关、20 uC/cm2 的残余极化以及高电阻状态和低电阻状态之间接近 1mV 的读出电压对比度。为了将器件物理与电路行为联系起来，我们开发并通过实验验证了一个紧凑的电路模型，该模型捕获自旋霍尔注入和自旋输运。使用优化材料参数进行的仿真预测输出电压 > 100mV，无需外部放大即可实现级联。使用该框架，我们设计了基于 MEMM 的存储器和逻辑块，包括 1T1R 阵列、两个逆变器实现（互补的两个器件和单器件）和一个三输入多数门，并评估深度流水线操作。该模型预计每次操作的开关能量降至 1 aJ，逻辑传播延迟为 30-60 ps，这表明 MEMM 是一个有前景的能量受限、高吞吐量计算平台。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.14031v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: We demonstrate a non-volatile magnetoelectric magnonic memory (MEMM) that enables fully electrical write/read via direct magnon-driven sensing in an insulating antiferromagnet. A fabricated SrIrO3/La-BiFeO3/SrIrO3 trilayer exhibits sub-100 ps switching, a remnant polarization of 20 uC/cm2, and a readout voltage contrast close to 1mV between high and low-resistance states. To connect device physics to circuit behavior, we develop and experimentally validate a compact circuit model that captures spin Hall injection and spin transport. Simulations with optimized material parameters predict output voltages > 100mV, enabling cascading without external amplification. Using this framework, we design MEMM-based memory and logic blocks, including a 1T1R array, two inverter implementations (complementary two-device and single-device), and a three-input majority gate, and evaluate deep-pipelined operation. The model projects switching energies down to 1 aJ per operation and logic propagation delays of 30-60 ps, indicating MEMM as a promising platform for energy-constrained, high throughput computing.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.14057v1 公告类型：新 摘要：我们报告了 Ba2La2CoTe2O12（S = 1/2 等边三角晶格反铁磁体，在低温下具有易平面各向异性）的 139La-NMR 研究。该化合物在 TN = 3.26 K 时经历磁相变，转变为具有 120 度自旋结构的有序状态。在3T以上的磁场下，TN分裂成TN1和TN2，分别对应于从顺磁相到上下(uud)相的转变以及从uud相到三角共面相的转变。 NMR 自旋晶格弛豫率 1/T1 在 TN1 处表现出临界发散，表明长程磁序的开始。在 TN2，在 5.4 T 处测量的 NMR 线宽表现出异常减小，我们将其归因于自旋结构从 uud 到三角形共面相的变化。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.14057v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: We report a 139La-NMR study of Ba2La2CoTe2O12, S = 1/2 equilateral triangular-lattice antiferromagnet with easy-plane anisotropy at low temperatures. This compound undergoes a magnetic phase transition at TN = 3.26 K into an ordered state with the 120 degree spin structure. Under magnetic fields above 3T, TN splits into TN1 and TN2, which correspond to the transitions from the paramagnetic phase to the up-up-down (uud) phase and from the uud phase to the triangular coplanar phase, respectively. The NMR spin-lattice relaxation rate 1/T1 exhibits a critical divergence at TN1, indicating the onset of long-range magnetic order. At TN2, the NMR-linewidth measured at 5.4 T exhibits an anomalous decrease, which we attribute to a change in the spin structure from the uud to the triangular coplanar phase.

页内定位所在专题
中文摘要

arXiv:2602.14133v1 公告类型：新 摘要：我们提出了 (111) 取向 (LaMnO₃₎₂ₙ|(SrMnO₃₎ₙ 超晶格中磁交换相互作用和临界行为的第一性原理研究，其中 n=2,4,6。对于所有正在研究的超晶格，我们发现强大的半金属铁磁性延伸到两个组成区域的所有层。研究发现，尽管确定了是否存在小 Jahn-Teller 畸变，但改变八面体倾斜模式对磁性的影响可以忽略不计。磁耦合对库仑相互作用参数变化的响应分析表明，铁磁性是由涉及巡回 e_g 电子的双交换机制驱动的，而其最终强度则因局域 t₂g 电子的超交换而受到反铁磁性贡献的阻碍。基于原子自旋动力学的多尺度模拟表明，最薄的超晶格 n=2,4 的有序温度至少与 La₂/₃Sr₁/₃MnO₃ 相当。相反，随着厚度的增加，出现两相行为，其中 SrMnO₃ 区域比 LaMnO₃ 区域更快地失去长程有序。虽然整体有序温度随着厚度的增加而增加，但我们认为观察到的两相行为的高温状态并不代表真实的物理系统，一旦长程有序在 SrMnO₃ 区域内丢失，该系统就会经历电子、磁和结构相变的组合。这项研究提供了对与氧化物异质结构相关的新兴磁性相和转变温度的见解。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.14133v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: We present a first-principles investigation of magnetic exchange interactions and critical behavior in (111)-oriented (LaMnO₃₎₂ₙ|(SrMnO₃₎ₙ superlattices for n=2,4,6. For all superlattices under investigation, we find robust half-metallic ferromagnetism extending across all the layers of both component regions. Changing octahedral tilt patterns is found to have negligible effects on the magnetic properties, despite determining the presence or absence of small Jahn-Teller distortions. The analysis of the response of the magnetic coupling to a variation of the Coulomb interaction parameters demonstrates that ferromagnetism is driven by a double-exchange mechanism involving itinerant e_g electrons, while its final strength is hampered by antiferromagnetic contributions due to the superexchange of localized t₂g electrons. Multi-scale simulations based on atomistic spin dynamics show that the thinnest superlattices, n=2,4, possess an ordering temperature that is at least comparable to that of La₂/₃Sr₁/₃MnO₃. Conversely, as thickness increases, a two-phase behavior emerges, where the SrMnO₃ region loses long-range order faster than the LaMnO₃ region. While the global ordering temperature increases together with thickness, we argue that the high-temperature regime for the observed two-phase behavior is not representative of the real physical system, which will undergo a combined electronic, magnetic and structural phase transition as soon as the long-range order is lost inside the SrMnO₃ region. This study provides insights into the emergent magnetic phases and transition temperatures relevant to oxide heterostructures.

arXiv:2602.14155v1 公告类型：新 摘要：手性磁体中的磁性斯格明子通常排列成六方晶格，其结构顺序受温度、外部磁场和几何约束等因素的影响。虽然斯格明子晶格中的平移缺陷（例如位错）已被广泛研究，但单个角度缺陷或向错仍然很大程度上未被探索。在这里，我们报告了使用聚焦离子束铣削制造的五边形和七边形 FeGe 纳米晶体中五倍和七倍向错的稳定性。在透射电子显微镜中使用菲涅尔成像和离轴电子全息术研究向错晶格的磁性和弹性结构。该结果得到了基于线弹性理论的微磁模拟和分析模型的支持。

English Abstract

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.14323v1 公告类型：新 摘要：我们在量子模拟器中实验研究了受抑自旋交换反铁磁体，该反铁磁体由排列成 kagome 阵列的 N = 114 个偶极里德伯原子组成。受最近无间隙 U(1) 狄拉克自旋液态基态理论提出的启发，我们使用局部寻址来绝热地准备低能态。我们通过这种绝热协议测量局部极化和自旋-自旋相关性，并观察我们的系统从交错的产物状态移动，通过中间磁性晶体，最后进入无序的相关液体。我们估计这种原子液体的熵密度与液氮温度下受挫磁绝缘体的熵密度相似。我们将液体中的相关性与狄拉克自旋液体的简单、无参数拟像的相关性进行比较，并发现符号结构和空间衰减具有良好的一致性。最后，我们探讨了系统对局部场扰动和几何畸变的静态敏感性。我们的结果确立了里德伯原子阵列作为量子自旋液体候选物的制备和微观表征的有前途的平台。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.14323v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: We experimentally investigate a frustrated spin-exchange antiferromagnet in a quantum simulator, composed of N = 114 dipolar Rydberg atoms arranged into a kagome array. Motivated by a recent theoretical proposal of a gapless U(1) Dirac spin liquid ground state, we use local addressing to adiabatically prepare low-energy states. We measure the local polarization and spin-spin correlations over this adiabatic protocol, and observe our system move from a staggered product state, through an intermediate magnetic crystal, and finally into a disordered, correlated liquid. We estimate the entropy density of this atomic liquid to be similar to that of frustrated magnetic insulators at liquid nitrogen temperatures. We compare the correlations in our liquid to those of a simple, parameter-free ansatz for the Dirac spin liquid, and find good agreement in the sign structure and spatial decay. Finally, we probe the static susceptibility of our system to a local field perturbation and to a geometrical distortion. Our results establish Rydberg atom arrays as a promising platform for the preparation and microscopic characterization of quantum spin liquid candidates.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.14377v1 公告类型：新 摘要：我们报告了通过低温拓扑化学 Ca²⁺/2Na⁺ 与 Na₂IrO₃ 交换，合成了与已知的后钙钛矿和钙钛矿相不同的 CaₓIrO₃ 钛铁矿型多晶型物。粉末 X 射线衍射可在 Rbar3 中进行索引，并且包括层滑移断层的整个图案建模表明，选择性加宽可以通过基于两个对称等效横向堆叠步骤之间的随机切换的一阶马尔可夫堆叠描述来捕获，具有明确的模型依赖性和至少几个百分点的不确定性。在 T^* sim 25 K（由 μ₀H = 10 mT 处 ZFC/FC 分叉的开始定义）处建议存在类似冻结的整体磁异常，并伴有广泛的热容特征和居里-魏斯行为，具有较大的负魏斯温度 θ_W sim -98 K。有效力矩 μₘ̊ ₑff = 1.68每个 Ir 的 μₘ̊ B 与 Ir⁴⁺ 的 Jₘ̊ ₑff = 1/2 一致。 SEM-EDX 表明 A 位含量低于 1 (Ca/Ir < 1)；因此，我们使用非化学计量公式 CaₓIrO₃ 来描述离子交换产物。这些结果将钛铁矿型 CaIrO₃ 确定为蜂窝状铱酸盐，其中堆积无序可以量化（需要注意模型和仪器相关性）并与其低温磁性行为相关。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.14377v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: We report the synthesis of an ilmenite-type polymorph of CaₓIrO₃ distinct from the known post-perovskite and perovskite phases, via low-temperature topochemical Ca²⁺/2Na⁺ exchange from Na₂IrO₃. Powder X-ray diffraction is indexable in Rbar3, and whole pattern modelling that includes layer glide faults indicates that the selective broadening can be captured by a first order Markov stacking description based on stochastic switching between two symmetry equivalent lateral stacking steps, with explicit model dependence and an uncertainty of at least several percent. A freezing-like bulk magnetic anomaly is suggested at T^* sim 25 K (defined by the onset of a ZFC/FC bifurcation at μ₀H = 10 mT), accompanied by a broad heat capacity feature and Curie-Weiss behavior with a large negative Weiss temperature of θ_W sim -98 K. The effective moment μₘ̊ ₑff = 1.68 μₘ̊ B per Ir is consistent with Jₘ̊ ₑff = 1/2 for an Ir⁴⁺. SEM-EDX suggests an A-site content below unity (Ca/Ir < 1); accordingly, we describe the ion-exchanged product using the nonstoichiometric formula CaₓIrO₃. These results identify ilmenite-type CaIrO₃ as a honeycomb iridate in which stacking disorder can be quantified (with caveats regarding model and instrument correlations) and related to its low-temperature magnetic behavior.

通过化学计量控制可逆调节应变 FeTe 薄膜中的磁序和本征超导性#

Reversible tuning of magnetic order and intrinsic superconductivity in strained FeTe thin films via stoichiometry control

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.14398v1 公告类型：新 摘要：FeTe 是铁基超导体的典型母体化合物。虽然块状 FeTe 是非超导的，具有长程双共线反铁磁序，但超导性已在薄膜中实现。然而，这些方法通常涉及复杂的氧掺入或界面效应，其微观机制仍然难以捉摸。在这里，我们在 SrTiO3 上制备了高纯度裸 FeTe 薄膜，并结合微观和宏观表征研究了它们的磁性和超导状态。通过减少间隙 Fe 杂质，我们成功地抑制了长程反铁磁有序，增强了准粒子相干性并在 ~10 K 下诱导了超导。此外，通过调节 Fe 浓度，该过程很容易可逆。我们的研究结果表明，精确的化学计量控制足以在应变 FeTe 薄膜中诱导本征超导性。这项工作提供了对铁硫属化物中磁性和超导性之间竞争的见解，并为开发稳定、高纯度的超导 FeTe 薄膜提供了一条可靠的途径。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.14398v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: FeTe is a prototypical parent compound of iron-based superconductors. While bulk FeTe is non-superconducting with a long-range bicollinear antiferromagnetic order, superconductivity has been achieved in thin films. However, the approaches usually involve complex oxygen incorporation or interfacial effects, the microscopic mechanisms of which remain elusive. Here, we prepare high-purity, bare FeTe thin films on SrTiO3 and investigate their magnetic and superconducting states combining both microscopic and macroscopic characterizations. By reducing the interstitial Fe impurities, we successfully suppress the long-range antiferromagnetic order, enhance the quasiparticle coherence and induce superconductivity at ~10 K. Moreover, this process is readily reversible by tuning the Fe concentration. Our findings reveal that precise stoichiometric control is sufficient to induce intrinsic superconductivity in strained FeTe thin films. This work provides insights into the competition between magnetism and superconductivity in iron chalcogenides, and supplies a robust pathway for developing stable, high-purity superconducting FeTe films.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.14429v1 发布类型：新 摘要：量化自旋轨道到电荷的转换效率对于自旋轨道电子学至关重要。两种广泛使用的确定这些效率的方法基于铁磁共振 (FMR)、用于逆效应的自旋泵 FMR 和用于直接效应的自旋扭矩 FMR。实现准确量化（尤其是自旋泵浦 FMR）的关键参数是 RF 场强度 hRF。我们提出了一个全面的理论模型和实验协议，可以正确量化 hRF。它经过了广泛的实验结果的验证，并在各种天线几何形状和铁磁系统中进行了严格的测试。我们证明，当 hRF 方向平行于铁磁表面时，奇对称洛伦兹电压（完美模拟自旋泵浦或自旋扭矩 FMR 信号）可以纯粹由整流效应（由于各向异性磁阻）产生。通过对各种 10 nm 厚的铁磁层（例如 Ni、NiFe、Fe 和 CoFeB）的系统研究，我们发现虽然 Fe 和 CoFeB 表现出最小的整流，但 Ni 和 NiFe 产生必须校正的强整流信号。我们进一步证明，对于铁磁厚度 łeq 6 nm，这些整流效应可以忽略不计，这在 NiFe/Pt 双层中得到了验证，为未来异质结构的设计提供了重要指导。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.14429v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Quantifying spin-orbital-to-charge conversion efficiency is crucial for spin-orbitronics. Two widely used methods for determining these efficiencies are based on ferromagnetic resonance (FMR), spin pumping FMR for the inverse effect, and spin-torque FMR for the direct effect. A key parameter to achieve accurate quantification, especially for spin-pumping FMR, is the RF field strength, hRF. We present a comprehensive theoretical model and experimental protocol that allow a correct quantification of hRF. It was validated by extensive experimental results and it was rigorously tested across various antennas geometries and ferromagnetic systems. We demonstrate that odd-symmetric Lorentzian voltages-which perfectly mimic spin-pumping or spin-torque FMR signals-can arise purely from rectification effects (due to anisotropic magnetoresistance) when hRF orientation is parallel to the ferromagnetic surface. Through a systematic study of various 10-nm-thick ferromagnetic layers, such as Ni, NiFe, Fe, and CoFeB, we find that while Fe and CoFeB exhibit minimal rectification, Ni and NiFe generate strong rectified signals that must be corrected. We further demonstrate that these rectification effects become negligible for ferromagnetic thicknesses łeq 6 nm, as validated in NiFe/Pt bilayers, providing an important guideline for the design of future heterostructures.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.14485v1 公告类型：新 摘要：传统超导性和非常规磁性之间的相互作用为实现奇异的超导现象提供了一个令人兴奋的平台。在这里，我们研究基于 CsV₂Te₂O 系列材料的平面和垂直结中的约瑟夫森效应，该材料具有 G 型反铁磁序的隐藏 d 波交变磁性。在基于单层的平面结中，互变磁体的准一维、近乎平坦的自旋极化带，当与s波超导体耦合时，产生具有强方向各向异性的完全自旋极化超电流——一种自旋选择性约瑟夫森效应。在多层结构中，我们发现了一种交替磁偶奇效应：自旋极化超电流仅在奇数层平面结中持续存在，但在偶数层中完全抵消。因此，层奇偶校验充当自旋极化超电流的开关。在垂直结中，奇数层势垒增强了等自旋三重态输运，而偶数层则有利于相反自旋输运，从而在总超流中随层数产生强大的第二周期振荡。这些依赖于层奇偶性的响应代表了隐藏交替磁体中的一般奇偶效应，适用于各种磁性和传输现象。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.14485v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: The interplay between conventional superconductivity and unconventional magnetism offers an exciting platform for realizing exotic superconducting phenomena. Here, we investigate Josephson effects in planar and vertical junctions based on CsV₂Te₂O-family materials, which host hidden d-wave altermagnetism with G-type antiferromagnetic order. In monolayer-based planar junctions, the quasi-1D, nearly flat, spin-polarized bands of the altermagnet, when coupled to s-wave superconductors, produce a fully spin-polarized supercurrent with strong directional anisotropy -- a spin-selective Josephson effect. In multilayers, we uncover an altermagnetic even-odd effect: spin-polarized supercurrents persist only in odd-layer planar junctions but cancel exactly in even layers. Thus, layer parity acts as a switch for spin-polarized supercurrent. In vertical junctions, odd-layer barriers enhance equal-spin triplet transport while even layers favor opposite-spin transport, yielding a robust period-two oscillation in the total supercurrent with layer number. These layer-parity-dependent responses represent a general even-odd effect in hidden altermagnets, applicable to diverse magnetic and transport phenomena.

arXiv:2602.14511v1 公告类型：新 摘要：利用量子距离，非相互作用极限下的磁化率可以严格分为两种贡献：一种仅由能带色散产生，另一种则源于量子几何贡献。在这封信中，我们将这种分解应用于两种材料：LaFeAsO 和 Pb₉Cu(PO₄₎₆O，并证明它们的主要磁涨落源自几何贡献。在LaFeAsO中，条带型反铁磁涨落主要源自量子几何，而在Pb₉Cu(PO₄₎₆O中，几何项抑制反铁磁涨落并稳定铁磁涨落。我们的研究结果强调了量子几何在控制多带系统磁涨落中的重要作用，并提供了一个独特的定量框架来解开通常被统称为多轨道效应的能带结构和波函数几何效应。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.14511v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Using quantum distance, magnetic susceptibility in the non-interacting limit can be rigorously split into two contributions: one arising solely from band dispersion, while the other stems from quantum geometric contributions. In this Letter, we apply this decomposition to two materials, LaFeAsO and Pb₉Cu(PO₄₎₆O, and demonstrate that their dominant magnetic fluctuations originate from the geometric contribution. In LaFeAsO, stripe-type antiferromagnetic fluctuations arise primarily from quantum geometry, while in Pb₉Cu(PO₄₎₆O the geometric term suppresses antiferromagnetic fluctuations and stabilizes ferromagnetic fluctuations. Our findings highlight the essential role of quantum geometry in governing magnetic fluctuations in multi-band systems, and provide a unique and quantitative framework to disentangle band-structure and wavefunction-geometry effects that have often been discussed collectively as multi-orbital effects.
