arXiv:2602.15073v1 公告类型：交叉 摘要：下一代引力波天文台（如 ET 和 CE）将检测具有高信噪比和长带内持续时间的 BNS 和 NSBH 吸气，使系统性预警警报既可行又具有科学价值。此类触发器对于协调快速电磁后续行动至关重要。在这项工作中，我们介绍了 GW-FALCON，这是一种新颖的特征驱动的深度学习框架，用于在下一代探测器中对 GW 信号+噪声和仅噪声数据进行早期检测。我们不是将原始时间序列输入 CNN 或更复杂的神经网络架构，而是首先使用 TSFEL 库从短观察时间窗口中提取大量统计、时间和光谱量。然后将所得的固定长度特征向量用作适合低延迟操作的前馈 ANN 的输入。我们使用模拟 BNS 和 NSBH 吸气波形来演示该方法，并将其注入由 ET 和 CE 设计 PSD 生成的有色高斯噪声中。我们在从部分吸气窗口中提取的特征集上训练单独的人工神经网络，这些特征集具有不同的最大瞬时频率，从而能够在合并前的数十到数百秒内触发预警。在所有检测器配置和数据集中，生成的分类器实现了高精度和检测效率，类 ET 网络通常达到 90% 的测试精度，类 CE 网络在低误报概率下超过 97%。据我们所知，这项工作为下一代引力波天文台提供了第一个基于特征的全面深度学习检测框架，将应变时间序列数据的特征提取与可扩展到实际数据和更先进的神经网络架构的设置中的鲁棒信号噪声分类连接起来。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.15073v1 Announce Type: cross Abstract: Next-generation GW observatories such as the ET and CE will detect BNS and NSBH inspirals with high SNRs and long in-band durations, making systematic early-warning alerts both feasible and scientifically valuable. Such triggers are essential for coordinating rapid electromagnetic follow-up. In this work, we introduce GW-FALCON, a novel feature-driven DL framework for early-time detection between GW signal+noise and noise-only data in next-generation detectors. Instead of feeding raw time series to CNN or more complex neural network architectures, we first extract a large set of statistical, temporal, and spectral quantities from short observational time windows using the TSFEL library. The resulting fixed-length feature vectors are then used as input to feed-forward ANNs suitable for low-latency operation. We demonstrate the method using simulated BNS and NSBH inspiral waveforms injected into colored Gaussian noise generated from the ET and CE design PSDs. We train separate ANNs on feature sets extracted from partial-inspiral windows characterized by different maximum instantaneous frequencies, enabling early-warning triggers from tens to hundreds of seconds before merger. Across all detector configurations and datasets, the resulting classifiers achieve high accuracy and detection efficiency, with ET-like networks typically reaching test accuracies of order 90% and CE-like ones exceeding 97% at low false-alarm probability. To the best of our knowledge, this work presents the first comprehensive feature-based DL detection framework for Next-generation GW observatories, connecting feature extraction from strain time series data to robust signal-noise classification within a setup that can be extended to real data and to more advanced neural network architectures.

中文摘要

arXiv:2504.01891v2 公告类型：替换 摘要：有效地理解和求解流体动力学方程仍然是计算物理学中的基本挑战。传统的数值求解器和基于物理的神经网络难以捕获偏微分方程解中的全部频率分量，从而限制了其准确性和效率。在这里，我们提出了多流物理混合网络，这是一种新颖的神经架构，它并行集成了量子层和经典层，以提高求解流体动力学方程（即“Kovasznay flow”问题）的准确性。这种方法将解决方案分解为单独的频率分量，每个分量都由独立的并行混合网络预测，从而简化了训练过程并提高了性能。我们在数据驱动和物理驱动的场景中针对可比较的经典神经网络（多流物理经典网络）评估了所提出的模型。我们的结果表明，与经典模型相比，多流物理混合网络的速度分量均方根误差降低了 36%，压力预测的均方根误差降低了 41%，同时使用的可训练参数减少了 24%。这些发现凸显了混合量子经典架构在推进计算流体动力学方面的潜力。

English Abstract

arXiv:2504.01891v2 Announce Type: replace Abstract: Understanding and solving fluid dynamics equations efficiently remains a fundamental challenge in computational physics. Traditional numerical solvers and physics-informed neural networks struggle to capture the full range of frequency components in partial differential equation solutions, limiting their accuracy and efficiency. Here, we propose the Multi-stream Physics Hybrid Network, a novel neural architecture that integrates quantum and classical layers in parallel to improve the accuracy of solving fluid dynamics equations, namely ''Kovasznay flow'' problem. This approach decomposes the solution into separate frequency components, each predicted by independent Parallel Hybrid Networks, simplifying the training process and enhancing performance. We evaluated the proposed model against a comparable classical neural network, the Multi-stream Physics Classical Network, in both data-driven and physics-driven scenarios. Our results show that the Multi-stream Physics Hybrid Network achieves a reduction in root mean square error by 36% for velocity components and 41% for pressure prediction compared to the classical model, while using 24% fewer trainable parameters. These findings highlight the potential of hybrid quantum-classical architectures for advancing computational fluid dynamics.

中文摘要

arXiv:2512.11895v2 公告类型：替换 摘要：这项工作提出了一种可解释的参数代理模型，其动机是需要识别用于实时解析物体轨迹的流体动力学模型。代理被公式化为规范配置的降阶模型，其中单自由度起伏球体在垂直壁附近运行。高保真 CFD 模拟用于生成不同壁距 (WD) 和跌落高度 (DH) 下的起伏衰减响应的参数数据集。然后，将非线性动力学稀疏辨识 (SINDy) 应用于每个 CFD 轨迹，以辨识低阶非线性常微分方程 (ODE)，其中多项式项代表有效静水力恢复和辐射阻尼，谐波项代表波引起的激振力。然后，将 SINDy 识别的系数用作神经算子网络 (ONet) 中的先验约束，该神经算子网络学习从壁距离和落差高度到 ODE 系数的平滑映射，从而生成能够预测输入空间中任意点的动力学的替代项，而无需重新运行昂贵的 CFD 计算。给出的限制假设下，生成的代理以接近最佳的精度再现 CFD 波浪衰减响应，同时能够实时运行。该方法为发射和回收操作的实时、基于物理的替代建模提供了一条实用途径。

English Abstract

arXiv:2512.11895v2 Announce Type: replace Abstract: This work presents an interpretable parametric surrogate model motivated by the need to identify a hydrodynamic model for resolving the trajectory of an object in real-time. The surrogate is formulated as a reduced-order model for a canonical configuration in which a one-degree-of-freedom heaving sphere operates near a vertical wall. High-fidelity CFD simulations are used to generate a parametric dataset of heave-decay responses over varying wall distances (WD) and drop heights (DH). Sparse Identification of Nonlinear Dynamics (SINDy) is then applied to each CFD trajectory to identify a low-order nonlinear ordinary differential equation (ODE) with polynomial terms representing effective hydrostatic restoring and radiation damping, and the harmonic terms representing the wave-induced excitation forces. The SINDy identified coefficients are then used as a prior constraint in a neural operator network (ONet) that learns a smooth mapping from wall distance and drop height to the ODE coefficients, yielding a surrogate capable of predicting dynamics at arbitrary points in the input space without rerunning expensive CFD calculations. The resulting surrogate reproduces CFD heave-decay responses with near-optimal accuracy given the limiting assumptions while being capable of running in real time. The approach provides a practical pathway toward real-time, physics-informed surrogate modelling for launch-and-recovery operations.

arXiv:2602.13725v1 公告类型：新 摘要：大正则蒙特卡罗 (GCMC) 模拟对于筛选用于气体吸附的金属有机框架 (MOF) 至关重要，但其准确性受到潜在原子间势的限制。通用机器学习原子间势（MLIP）在不同的化学数据集上进行训练，无需系统特定的训练即可实现零样本预测。我们引入了MLIP-MC，这是一个开源Python框架，可以使用MLIP进行GCMC模拟，并使用该框架对一系列通用模型进行基准测试，包括MACE-MP-0、ORB-v3和fairchem ODAC，用于ZIF-8、ZIF-4和Mg-MOF-74上的CO2吸附。所有通用模型都表现出系统偏差，始终高估或低估吸附能量。至关重要的是，准确性取决于训练数据的组成：只有经过 MOF-吸附物相互作用训练的模型才能与密度泛函理论得出的参考达到合理的一致性。误差随着 CO2 吸收呈线性增长，反映了吸附物-吸附物相互作用中的复合误差。我们的结果表明，当前的通用 MLIP 需要进行定量吸附预测的微调，并证明 MLIP-MC 快速测试模型的能力。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.13725v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Grand canonical Monte Carlo (GCMC) simulations are essential for screening metal-organic frameworks (MOFs) for gas adsorption, yet their accuracy is limited by underlying interatomic potentials. Universal machine-learned interatomic potentials (MLIPs), trained on diverse chemical datasets, promise zero-shot prediction without system-specific training. We introduce MLIP-MC, an open-source Python framework to conduct GCMC simulations with MLIPs, and use this framework to benchmark a series of universal models, including MACE-MP-0, ORB-v3, and fairchem ODAC, for CO2 adsorption on ZIF-8, ZIF-4, and Mg-MOF-74. All universal models exhibit systematic biases, consistently over- or underestimating adsorption energetics. Crucially, accuracy depends on training data composition: only models trained on MOF-adsorbate interactions achieve reasonable agreement with a density functional theory derived reference. Errors grow linearly with CO2 uptake, reflecting compounding inaccuracies in adsorbate-adsorbate interactions. Our results demonstrate that current universal MLIPs require finetuning for quantitative adsorption predictions and demonstrate the power of MLIP-MC to rapidly test models.

arXiv:2602.13911v1 公告类型：新 摘要：预测将胶体颗粒桥接成瞬态网络的缔合聚合物的流变行为从根本上具有挑战性，因为耦合的时空尺度阻碍了有效的分子保真度建模。我们通过一个新颖的、统一的多尺度模拟框架来解决这个问题，该框架用于遥爪聚合物胶体悬浮液，集成了：显式链布朗动力学解决聚合物-颗粒缔合动力学；主动学习元模型将动力学压缩为有效的替代物；人口平衡-布朗动力学（Pop-BD）根据元模型预测计算网络规模动态。我们的框架经过显式链布朗动力学验证，可以准确地再现时间和频率相关的应力松弛模量，从而能够在更长的时间尺度上模拟更大的系统。系统研究表明，网络连通性在特定的链与粒子比率下表现出关键转变，键密度和寿命与增强的弛豫时间和模量相关。颗粒体积分数越高，键合越持久，弛豫速度越慢。该框架将链级动力学与宏观流变学联系起来，从而能够对水性涂料和软物质应用的缔合胶体材料进行高效、合理的计算设计。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.13911v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Predicting the rheological behavior of associative polymers bridging colloidal particles into transient networks is fundamentally challenging because the coupled spatiotemporal scales prevent efficient molecular-fidelity modeling. We address this through a novel, unified multiscale simulation framework for telechelic polymer-colloid suspensions integrating: explicit-chain Brownian dynamics resolving polymer-particle association kinetics; active learning metamodels compressing kinetics into efficient surrogates; and Population Balance-Brownian Dynamics (Pop-BD) computing network-scale dynamics from metamodel predictions. Validated against explicit-chain Brownian dynamics, our framework accurately reproduces time-and frequency-dependent stress relaxation moduli, enabling simulations of larger systems over longer timescales. Systematic investigations reveal that network connectivity exhibits critical transitions at specific chain-to-particle ratios, with bond density and lifetime correlating to enhanced relaxation times and moduli. Higher particle volume fractions yield more persistent bonds and slower relaxation. This framework connects chain-level dynamics to macroscopic rheology, enabling computationally efficient rational design of associative colloidal materials for waterborne coatings and soft-matter applications.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.14603v1 公告类型：新 摘要：溶质在界面上的分离会显着影响材料行为。绝大多数理论工作都集中在晶界和相干界面上。对半相干界面的研究通常因结构复杂性而被禁止，产生的模型超出了密度泛函理论（DFT）的实际能力，或化学复杂性，受到（经典）原子间势的可用性的限制。这项工作利用新型通用机器学习原子间势（uMLIP）研究了珠光体中相干和半相干 α-Fe/Fe₃C 界面的溶质偏析及其对机械性能的影响。 DFT 计算的溶液焓、偏析能量和相干界面内聚力的变化用于对几种最先进的 uMLIP 进行基准测试。我们发现 GRACE-2L-OAM 和 GRACE-2L-OMAT 模型最准确地再现了量子力学预测。虽然 Cu 对所研究的杂质元素和微量元素之间的相干界面具有最强的偏析能，为 approx -0.3 eV，但在半相干界面存在失配位错的情况下，所有元素（As、Cr、Cu、Mo、Ni、P、Sb 和 Sn）都表现出明显更高的负偏析值，达到 approx -1.5 eV 以下。尽管溶质种类之间偏析能的空间分布明显不同，但在位错核心附近发现了最深的陷阱。 Sb、Sn、P 和 As 强烈降低共格界面的内聚力，而 Cu 仅轻微降低共格界面的内聚力，而 Ni 的影响可忽略不计，Cr 和 Mo 略微增强内聚力。相比之下，所有研究的溶质（P 除外）都倾向于使半共格界面脆化，其中 Sn，尤其是 Sb 在面外方向进行的拉伸测试中具有最强的影响。 ArXiv 的摘要被缩短。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.14603v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Solute segregation to interfaces significantly impacts material behavior. A large majority of theoretical works focus on grain boundaries and coherent interfaces. Studies on semi-coherent interfaces are usually prohibited by the structural complexity, yielding models beyond the practical capability of density functional theory (DFT), or chemical complexity, restricted by the availability of (classical) interatomic potentials. This work investigates solute segregation to the coherent and semi-coherent α-Fe/Fe₃C interface in pearlite and its effect on mechanical properties using novel universal machine learning interatomic potentials (uMLIPs). DFT calculated solution enthalpies, segregation energetics, and changes in cohesion at the coherent interface are used to benchmark several state-of-the-art uMLIPs. We find that the GRACE-2L-OAM and GRACE-2L-OMAT models most accurately reproduce the quantum-mechanical predictions. While Cu has the strongest segregation energy of approx -0.3 eV to the coherent interface among the investigated tramp and trace elements, all of them, As, Cr, Cu, Mo, Ni, P, Sb, and Sn, exhibit significantly more negative segregation values reaching below approx -1.5 eV in the presence of the misfit dislocation at the semi-coherent interface. The deepest traps are identified in the vicinity of the dislocation core, although the spatial distribution of segregation energies differs markedly among the solute species. The cohesion of the coherent interface is strongly reduced by Sb, Sn, P, and As, and only mildly by Cu, whereas Ni shows a negligible effect, and Cr and Mo slightly enhance cohesion. In contrast, all investigated solutes (except for P) tend to embrittle the semi-coherent interface, with Sn and, especially, Sb having the strongest impact in tensile tests performed in the out-of-plane direction. Abstract shortened for ArXiv.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.14650v1 发布类型：新 摘要：机器学习模型越来越多地应用于材料科学，但其预测能力往往受到数据稀缺的限制。在这里，我们表明，即使训练样本数量有限，只要数据集紧凑并且基于物理相关量，就可以实现准确的预测。通过将密度泛函理论计算与机器学习框架相结合，我们构建了精确的基于描述符的模型来预测掺杂纤铁矿 TiO₂ 单层的形成能。首先针对单掺杂 Pt 配置评估了机器学习模型的预测准确性，证明所选的结构和化学描述符可靠地捕获了控制掺杂稳定性的关键因素。然后通过扩展数据集以包括掺银配置来检查化学可转移性。随着训练中包含额外的掺银数据点，预测准确性得到系统性提高，同时 Pt 的性能仍然保持稳健。这些结果凸显了小型且精心策划的数据集与物理信息描述符相结合的潜力，不仅可以在掺杂的 TiO₂ 单层中实现准确且可化学转移的机器学习驱动筛选。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.14650v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Machine learning models are increasingly applied in materials science, yet their predictive power is often constrained by data scarcity. Here, we show that accurate predictions can be achieved, even with a limited number of training examples, provided the dataset is compact and and grounded in physically relevant quantities. By combining density functional theory calculations with a machine-learning framework, we construct accurate descriptor-based models to predict the formation energies of doped lepidocrocite TiO₂ monolayers. The predictive accuracy of machine-learning models was first evaluated for single-dopant Pt configurations, demonstrating that the selected structural and chemical descriptors reliably capture the key factors governing dopant stability. Chemical transferability is then examined by extending the dataset to include Ag-doped configurations. Predictive accuracy improved systematically as additional Ag-doped data points were included in the training, while the performance of Pt remains robust. These results highlight the potential of small and well-curated datasets combined with physically informed descriptors to enable not only accurate but also chemically transferable machine-learning-driven screening in doped TiO₂ monolayer.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.14867v1 公告类型：新 摘要：我们报告了一种新颖的混合方法，可以对关键区域（接触表面、裂纹区域等）中的固体进行同步原子模拟，以及其他零件的连续介质建模。连续体按照不同尺寸的准原子进行处理，包括复合介质。准原子之间的相互作用势参数经过优化，以使复合介质的弹性特性与原子介质的弹性特性相匹配。该优化方法在概念上与在线机器学习（ML）方法一致，使其计算效率非常高。这种方法允许直接应用分子动力学 (MD) 标准软件包，并辅以基于 ML 的优化器。新方法适用于具有简单的成对 Lennard-Jones 势以及描述共价键的多体 Tersoff 势的模型系统。使用 LAMMPS 软件我们模拟不同尺寸颗粒的碰撞。通过将新方法获得的模拟结果与全原子模拟进行比较，我们证明了其准确性、有效性和计算速度方面的压倒性优势。此外，我们将我们的方法与其他混合方法进行比较，特别是与最接近的方法——AtC（原子到连续体）方法。我们展示了我们的方法在计算速度和实施便利性方面的显着优势。最后，我们讨论了对其他现象进行建模的方法的可能扩展。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.14867v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: We report a novel hybrid method of simultaneous atomistic simulation of solids in critical regions (contacts surfaces, cracks areas, etc.), along with continuum modeling of other parts. The continuum is treated in terms of quasi-atoms of different size, comprising composite medium. The parameters of interaction potential between the quasi-atoms are optimized to match elastic properties of the composite medium to those of the atomic one. The optimization method coincides conceptually with the online Machine Learning (ML) methods, making it computationally very efficient. Such an approach allows a straightforward application of standard software packages for molecular dynamics (MD), supplemented by the ML-based optimizer. The new method is applied to model systems with a simple, pairwise Lennard-Jones potential, as well with multi-body Tersoff potential, describing covalent bonds. Using LAMMPS software we simulate collision of particles of different size. Comparing simulation results, obtained by the novel method, with full-atomic simulations, we demonstrate its accuracy, validity and overwhelming superiority in computational speed. Furthermore, we compare our method with other hybrid methods, specifically, with the closest one -- AtC (Atomic to Continuum) method. We demonstrate a significant superiority of our approach in computational speed and implementation convenience. Finally, we discuss a possible extension of the method for modeling other phenomena.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.15002v1 公告类型：新 摘要：跨平面热传输是范德华 (vdW) 电子学的关键瓶颈，但其微观控制原理仍然难以捉摸。我们证明，堆叠顺序是多层二硫化铼（ReS2）中跨平面声子传输的有效控制旋钮。与厚度相关的热导率测量揭示了非常长的跨平面声子平均自由程 (MFP) (>= 200-300 nm)，并提供了从准弹道输运到与厚度无关的弹道极限转变的直接实验观察。 AA 堆叠的横截面热导率几乎是 AB 堆叠的两倍，这是由更“相干”的层间记录带来的更长的声学声子寿命驱动的。集成的深度神经网络分子动力学揭示了 ReS2 中的声子滤波从根本上来说是频率选择性的：弱 vdW 耦合充当低通滤波器，而更强的耦合则拓宽了传输通带。这些结果将 ReS2 确立为一个模型系统，可以通过设计堆叠顺序和层间耦合来调节扩散、准弹道和弹道区域的热传导，为二维电子学中的热管理提供新的框架。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.15002v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Cross-plane heat transport is a critical bottleneck for van der Waals (vdW) electronics, yet its microscopic governing principles remain elusive. We demonstrate that stacking order is an effective control knob for cross-plane phonon transport in multilayer Rhenium Disulfide (ReS2). Thickness-dependent thermal conductivity measurements reveal remarkably long cross-plane phonon mean free paths (MFPs) (>= 200-300 nm) and provide a direct experimental observation of the transition from quasi-ballistic transport to a thickness-independent ballistic limit. AA stacking exhibits nearly double the cross-plane thermal conductivity of AB stacking, driven by longer acoustic phonon lifetimes from a more "coherent" interlayer registry. Integrated deep neural-network molecular dynamics reveals that phonon filtering in ReS2 is fundamentally frequency-selective: weak vdW coupling acts as a low-pass filter, whereas stronger coupling broadens the transmission passband. These results establish ReS2 as a model system where stacking order and interlayer coupling can be engineered to tune heat conduction across diffusive, quasi-ballistic, and ballistic regimes, offering a new framework for thermal management in 2D electronics.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.13257v1 公告类型：cross 摘要：蜂窝超材料为定制非线性机械响应提供了广阔的设计空间，但使用传统建模方法探索该空间通常是不可行或不可扩展的。为了充分利用它们的非线性行为进行逆向设计，有必要学习完整的应力-应变响应，而不是依赖大量的量，从而促进使用神经算子进行函数到函数的映射。然而，超材料非线性响应的数据驱动建模受到昂贵实验数据有限的严重限制。在这里，我们提出了一种贝叶斯多保真深度算子网络，该网络将丰富的低保真有限元模拟与来自旋节线超材料原位纳米力学实验的稀疏高保真实验数据聚合起来，从而实现异构信息聚合。引入混合贝叶斯主动学习策略，通过共同最大化微观结构的认知不确定性和几何多样性来选择信息样本，从而大大降低 3D 非线性模拟的成本。这种方法自适应地训练低保真算子，然后通过高保真贝叶斯残差学习器对其进行增强。我们证明，与高保真基线相比，仅从 3000 个设计池中战略性选择的 22 个样本就足以实现 MSE 降低 84.1%。该框架的性能显着优于单保真度基线，为完全非线性应力应变响应以及刚度、强度和能量吸收提供了卓越的预测。这项工作为细胞超材料的逆向设计和本构建模提供了一条稳健、数据高效的途径。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.13257v1 Announce Type: cross Abstract: Cellular metamaterials offer a vast design space for tailoring nonlinear mechanical responses, yet exploring this space with conventional modeling approaches is often infeasible or not scalable. To fully exploit their nonlinear behavior for inverse design, it is essential to learn the full stress-strain response rather than relying on bulk quantities, motivating the use of neural operators for function-to-function mapping. However, data-driven modeling of nonlinear response for metamaterials is severely constrained by the limited availability of costly experimental data. Here, we propose a Bayesian multi-fidelity deep operator network that aggregates abundant low-fidelity finite element simulations with sparse high-fidelity experimental data from in-situ nanomechanical experiments on spinodal metamaterials, enabling heterogeneous information aggregation. A hybrid Bayesian active learning strategy is introduced to select informative samples by jointly maximizing epistemic uncertainty and geometric diversity of the microstructure, substantially reducing the cost of 3D nonlinear simulations. This approach adaptively trains the low-fidelity operator, which is then augmented by a high-fidelity Bayesian residual learner. We demonstrate that only 22 strategically selected samples from a design pool of 3000 are sufficient to achieve an 84.1 percent reduction in MSE compared to the high-fidelity baseline. The framework significantly outperforms single-fidelity baselines, providing superior predictions for full nonlinear stress-strain responses as well as stiffness, strength, and energy absorption. This work provides a robust, data-efficient pathway for the inverse design and constitutive modeling of cellular metamaterials.

中文摘要

arXiv:2509.20164v2 公告类型：替换 摘要：低维材料具有吸引人的特性，推动了新材料发现的巨大努力。然而，实验对于系统发现来说是乏味的，并且现有的计算方法通常针对二维（2D）材料，而忽略了其他低维材料。在这里，我们结合了通用机器学习原子间势（UMLIP）和先进的、基于原子间力常数（FC）的维度分类方法，大量发现了新型低维材料。我们首先对 UMLIP 在量化 FC 方面的第一原理级精度进行了基准测试，并计算了材料项目数据库中 35,689 种材料的声子。然后，我们使用基于 FC 的方法进行维数分类，发现了 9139 种低维材料，其中包括 1838 个 0D 簇、1760 个一维链、3057 个 2D 片/层和 2484 种混合维材料，所有这些都是传统几何描述符无法识别的。通过计算已发现的二维材料的结合能，我们还确定了 887 个可以轻松或潜在地从其母体结构剥离的片材。

English Abstract

arXiv:2509.20164v2 Announce Type: replace Abstract: Low-dimensional materials have attractive properties that drive intense efforts for novel materials discovery. However, experiments are tedious for systematic discovery, and present computational methods are often tuned to two-dimensional (2D) materials, overlooking other low-dimensional materials. Here, we combined universal machine-learning interatomic potentials (UMLIPs) and an advanced, interatomic force constant (FC) -based dimensionality classification method to make a massive discovery of novel low-dimensional materials. We first benchmarked UMLIPs' first-principles-level accuracy in quantifying FCs and calculated phonons for 35,689 materials from the Materials Project database. We then used the FC-based method for dimensionality classification to discover 9139 low-dimensional materials, including 1838 0D clusters, 1760 1D chains, 3057 2D sheets/layers, and 2484 mixed-dimensionality materials, all of which conventional geometric descriptors have not recognized. By calculating the binding energies for the discovered 2D materials, we also identified 887 sheets that could be easily or potentially exfoliated from their parent bulk structures.

修复 pimd/langevin：LAMMPS 中路径积分分子动力学的有效实现#

fix pimd/langevin: An Efficient Implementation of Path Integral Molecular Dynamics in LAMMPS

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.13553v1 公告类型：新 摘要：路径积分分子动力学 (PIMD) 将量子粒子映射到虚构的环状聚合物经典系统上，并使用分子动力学传播此扩展经典系统的“珠子”，广泛用于捕获分子模拟中的核量子效应 (NQE)。准确的 PIMD 计算通常需要大量珠子，因此计算要求较高。虽然 i-PI 等软件包提供了全面的 PIMD 功能，但由机器学习原子间势（例如深势 (DP)）驱动的模拟的高效率需要更高效的 PIMD 实现，以充分利用现代大规模并行超级计算机。在这里，我们介绍修复 pimd/langevin，这是 LAMMPS 中的高效 PIMD 实现，它支持常用功能并利用 LAMMPS 的消息传递接口架构来实现高计算效率。我们使用液态水作为代表性示例来演示用法并验证代码的正确性，并提供支持的功能的全面概述。然后我们讨论实现的几个重要的技术方面。使用水的 DP 模拟作为基准，我们表明与 i-PI 相比，我们的实现实现了数倍的加速。最后，我们报告强和弱的扩展结果，证明我们的代码具有良好的并行性能。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.13553v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Path integral molecular dynamics (PIMD), which maps a quantum particle onto a fictitious classical system of ring polymers and propagates the "beads" of this extended classical system using molecular dynamics, is widely used to capture nuclear quantum effects (NQEs) in molecular simulations. Accurate PIMD calculations typically require a large number of beads and are therefore computationally demanding. While software packages such as i-PI offer comprehensive PIMD functionality, the high efficiency of simulations driven by machine learning interatomic potentials, such as Deep Potential (DP), calls for more efficient PIMD implementations that fully exploit modern massively parallel supercomputers. Here we present fix pimd/langevin, an efficient PIMD implementation in LAMMPS that supports commonly used features and leverages the Message Passing Interface architecture of LAMMPS to achieve high computational efficiency. We demonstrate the usage and validate the correctness of our code using liquid water as a representative example, and provide a comprehensive overview of the supported features. Then we discuss several important technical aspects of the implementation. Using DP simulations of water as a benchmark, we show that our implementation achieves several-fold acceleration compared to i-PI. Finally, we report strong and weak scaling results that demonstrate the favorable parallel performance of our code.

arXiv:2602.13601v1 公告类型：新 摘要：将物理上真实的 Lennard Jones LJ 势集成到直接模拟蒙特卡罗 DSMC 中长期以来一直受到评估详细散射动力学的高成本的阻碍。我们提出了一个高保真、机器学习加速的框架，该框架将严格的分子物理和大规模动力学模拟联系起来，并在 Bird 标准 DSMC 算法套件中实现。将 LJ 一致特性纳入 DSMC 总横截面公式中，并用替代模型取代昂贵的粒子散射步骤，解决了两个挑战。首先，我们通过局部粘度匹配开发了通用的可变有效直径模型，捕获了较宽温度范围内的吸引排斥相互作用，这比仅限于窄热带的传统模型有所进步。其次，我们采用深度算子网络作为 LJ 散射积分的快速、准确替代品，从而实现高效的高精度碰撞。由此产生的框架揭示了标准模型经常忽略的物理效应，并在三个典型问题上进行了验证：氦气和氩气中的冲击波、具有低温壁的超音速库埃特流以及两马赫数的高超音速圆柱流。在氩气冲击情况下，我们表明，虽然可变硬球 VHS 模型无法匹配实验密度分布，但其速度分布函数紧密遵循 LJ 预测。在低温超音速库埃特流中，LJ 模型预测的剪切应力比 VHS 更小，强调了低温剪切层中远程吸引力的主导影响。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.13601v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Integrating a physically realistic Lennard Jones LJ potential into Direct Simulation Monte Carlo DSMC has long been hindered by the high cost of evaluating detailed scattering dynamics. We present a high-fidelity, machine-learning-accelerated framework that bridges rigorous molecular physics and large-scale kinetic simulation, implemented within Bird standard DSMC algorithm suite. Two challenges are solved incorporating LJ consistent properties into DSMC total cross-section formulation, and replacing the expensive particle scattering step with a surrogate model. First, we develop a universal Variable Effective Diameter model via local viscosity matching, capturing attractive repulsive interactions over a wide temperature range an advance over traditional models restricted to narrow thermal bands. Second, we employ a Deep Operator Network as a fast, accurate substitute for the LJ scattering integral, enabling efficient high-precision collisions. The resulting framework exposes physical effects often missed by standard models and is validated on three canonical problems: shock waves in helium and argon, supersonic Couette flow with cryogenic walls, and hypersonic cylinder flow at two Mach numbers. In the argon shock case, we show that while the Variable Hard Sphere VHS model fails to match the experimental density profile, its velocity distribution function closely follows the LJ prediction. In low temperature supersonic Couette flow, the LJ model predicts smaller shear stress than VHS, underscoring the dominant influence of long-range attractive forces in cryogenic shear layers.

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.13893v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: The design of high-performance optical systems remains a specialized domain gated by the limited availability of expert engineers, creating a bottleneck that stalls innovation despite the growing demand for imaging hardware. While deep learning has improved parameter optimization, it has yet to address the fundamental challenge of conceptualizing valid optical architectures from functional requirements. Here, we present an end-to-end generative framework that couples the semantic reasoning of Large Language Models (LLMs) with a differentiable ray-tracing engine to democratize the synthesis of diffraction-limited optical prescriptions. By treating optical design as a semantic-to-physical translation task, the system autonomously interprets prompts ranging from high-level end-user requests to rigorous technical specifications. We demonstrate the framework's versatility across three distinct regimes: (1) finite-conjugate industrial metrology systems, where the model autonomously enforces application-specific constraints such as telecentricity to achieve diffraction-limited performance; (2) a suite of infrared objectives (NIR, SWIR, and LWIR), demonstrating the framework's ability to synthesize valid topologies and optical prescriptions for non-visible spectral bands, and (3) complex aspheric mobile lenses, where the system successfully navigates the high-dimensional optimization landscape to produce high-resolution designs suitable for modern sensors. Validated against industry-standard simulation tools, these results establish a new paradigm for automated optical engineering, bridging the gap between semantic intent and physical realization.

arXiv:2602.14022v1 发布类型：新 摘要：机器学习势（MLP）已成为现代分子模拟的重要工具。然而，开发同时实现高精度和高计算效率的模型仍然是一个重大挑战。在这项工作中，我们通过将基于单体的能量分解、置换不变多项式（PIP）描述符和基于碎片的策略中的神经网络相结合，将最近提出的 MB-PIPNet 框架扩展到一般的共价键分子系统。在此框架内，总势能表示为有效单体贡献的总和，其中 PIP 提供了单体内部结构及其局部化学环境的紧凑且化学驱动的描述。作为概念验证应用程序，我们将 MB-PIPNet 框架应用于线性烷烃，使用正十四烷作为代表系统，并根据已建立的原子机器学习模型对其性能进行基准测试。由此产生的 MB-PIPNet 势能准确地再现参考从头开始电子能量，并可靠地捕获关键分子特性，包括从分子动力学模拟获得的扭转势能分布、简谐振动频率和振动功率谱。重要的是，与其他 MLP 模型相比，MB-PIPNet 在能量和力的组合评估方面表现出计算效率的巨大优势。这些结果将 MB-PIPNet 确立为构建 MLP 的可扩展且高效的框架，为复杂分子系统的大规模量子和经典模拟提供了额外的途径。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.14022v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Machine-learning potentials (MLPs) have become important tools for modern molecular simulations. However, developing models that simultaneously achieve high accuracy and high computational efficiency remains a significant challenge. In this work, we extend the recently proposed MB-PIPNet framework to general covalently bonded molecular systems by combining monomer-based energy decomposition, permutationally invariant polynomial (PIP) descriptors, and neural networks within a fragmentation-based strategy. Within this framework, the total potential energy is represented as a sum of effective monomeric contributions, where PIPs provide compact and chemically motivated descriptions of both monomer internal structures and their local chemical environments. As a proof-of-concept application, we apply the MB-PIPNet framework to linear alkanes, using n-Tetradecane as a representative system, and benchmark its performance against established atomistic machine-learning models. The resulting MB-PIPNet potential accurately reproduces reference ab initio electronic energies and reliably captures key molecular properties, including torsional potential energy profiles, harmonic vibrational frequencies, and vibrational power spectra obtained from molecular dynamics simulations. Importantly, MB-PIPNet demonstrates a substantial advantage in computational efficiency over other MLP models for combined energy and force evaluations. These results establish MB-PIPNet as a scalable and efficient framework for constructing MLPs, providing an additional route for large-scale quantum and classical simulations of complex molecular systems.

arXiv:2602.14531v1 公告类型：新 摘要：粗粒度分子动力学通常会为了计算效率而牺牲准确性和可转移性，但机器学习势的使用正在帮助粗粒度模型获得与原子分子动力学相当的性能。然而，由于广泛使用的“自下而上”粗粒度目标的极端数据需求，开发粗粒度势能面的表示面临着严峻的缩放挑战。在这项工作中，我们表明，平均力匹配是一种训练热力学一致的粗粒度模型的策略，需要的训练样本数量减少了 50 倍，总原子模拟时间减少了 87%，同时与其他常用目标相比，在未见蛋白质的平均力潜力方面获得了更高的准确性。通过系统地消除目标函数中的噪声，我们证明可以扩展粗粒度的机器学习架构，从而实现高精度和可转移的模型。我们从理论上和通过使用热力学一致性作为主要精度指标的详尽基准测试来展示平均力匹配的优点。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.14531v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Coarse-grained molecular dynamics often sacrifices accuracy and transferability for computational efficiency, but the use of machine learned potentials is helping coarse-grained models attain performance on par with atomistic molecular dynamics. Nevertheless, developing representations of the coarse-grained potential energy surface faces severe scaling challenges due to the extreme data demands of widely used "bottom-up" coarse-graining objectives. In this work, we show that mean force matching, a strategy for training thermodynamically consistent coarse-grained models, requires 50x fewer training samples and 87% less total atomistic simulation time, while obtaining better accuracy on the potential of mean force for unseen proteins compared to other commonly used objectives. By systematically removing noise from the objective function, we demonstrate that it is possible to scale machine learning architectures for coarse-graining, enabling highly accurate and transferable models. We show the advantages of mean force matching both theoretically and through exhaustive benchmarking using thermodynamic consistency as the primary metric of accuracy.

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.14918v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: High-resolution fluid simulations for plasma physics and astrophysics rely on Particle in cell (PIC) and hydrodynamic solvers (e.g., FLASH) to resolve shock dominated, multiscale phenomena, but their high computational cost severely limits scalability. By incorporating weak physics constraints derived from the Euler equations using finite difference method, the model captures the self similar shock evolution and associated flow structures without explicitly solving the full hydrodynamic equations at each timestep. Comparing to the baseline MeshGraphNet model, PhyMGN is able to generalize beyond the training regime with a higher accuracy and preserves differentiability in parameter space while achieving a substantial reduction in computational cost relative to conventional numerical solvers.

页内定位所在专题
中文摘要

arXiv:2602.14975v1 公告类型：新 摘要：继我们之前的工作 (J. Phys. Chem. Lett., 2026, 17, 5, 1288-1295) 后，我们提出了 DMTS-NC 方法，这是一种使用非保守 (NC) 力的蒸馏多时间步长 (DMTS) 策略，使用基础神经网络模型进一步加速原子分子动力学模拟。在那里，双级可逆参考系统传播器算法（RESPA）形式将目标准确的保守势与针对非保守力的产生而优化的简化蒸馏表示相结合。尽管是非保守的，但蒸馏架构旨在强制执行关键的物理先验，例如旋转下的等变性和原子力分量的抵消。这些选择促进了蒸馏过程，因此极大地提高了模拟的鲁棒性，显着限制了更简单势能中的“漏洞”，从而与力数据实现了良好的一致性。总体而言，DMTS-NC 方案比保守的方案更稳定、更高效，并且比 DMTS 的额外加速达到 15-30%。不需要微调步骤，更容易实施，并且可以将系统物理共振推至极限，以保持精度，同时提供最大效率。至于 DMTS，DMTS-NC 适用于任何神经网络潜力。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.14975v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Following our previous work (J. Phys. Chem. Lett., 2026, 17, 5, 1288-1295), we propose the DMTS-NC approach, a distilled multi-time-step (DMTS) strategy using non conservative (NC) forces to further accelerate atomistic molecular dynamics simulations using foundation neural network models. There, a dual-level reversible reference system propagator algorithm (RESPA) formalism couples a target accurate conservative potential to a simplified distilled representation optimized for the production of non-conservative forces. Despite being non-conservative, the distilled architecture is designed to enforce key physical priors, such as equivariance under rotation and cancellation of atomic force components. These choices facilitate the distillation process and therefore improve drastically the robustness of simulation, significantly limiting the "holes" in the simpler potential, thus achieving excellent agreement with the forces data. Overall, the DMTS-NC scheme is found to be more stable and efficient than its conservative counterpart with additional speedups reaching 15-30% over DMTS. Requiring no finetuning steps, it is easier to implement and can be pushed to the limit of the systems physical resonances to maintain accuracy while providing maximum efficiency. As for DMTS, DMTS-NC is applicable to any neural network potential.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.13805v1 公告类型：cross 摘要：未经训练的神经网络 (UNN) 提供高保真电磁逆散射重建，但在计算上受到高维空间域优化的限制。我们提出了一种实时物理驱动的傅里叶谱（PDF）求解器，通过谱域降维实现亚秒级重建。通过使用截断傅立叶基扩展感应电流，优化被限制在散射测量支持的紧凑低频参数空间内。该求解器集成了收缩积分方程 (CIE) 以减轻高对比度非线性，并集成了对比度补偿算子 (CCO) 以校正光谱引起的衰减。此外，还制定了桥抑制损耗以增强相邻散射体之间的边界锐度。数值和实验结果表明，与最先进的 UNN 相比，速度提高了 100 倍，并且在噪声和天线不确定性下具有强大的性能，从而实现了实时微波成像应用。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.13805v1 Announce Type: cross Abstract: Untrained neural networks (UNNs) offer high-fidelity electromagnetic inverse scattering reconstruction but are computationally limited by high-dimensional spatial-domain optimization. We propose a Real-Time Physics-Driven Fourier-Spectral (PDF) solver that achieves sub-second reconstruction through spectral-domain dimensionality reduction. By expanding induced currents using a truncated Fourier basis, the optimization is confined to a compact low-frequency parameter space supported by scattering measurements. The solver integrates a contraction integral equation (CIE) to mitigate high-contrast nonlinearity and a contrast-compensated operator (CCO) to correct spectral-induced attenuation. Furthermore, a bridge-suppressing loss is formulated to enhance boundary sharpness between adjacent scatterers. Numerical and experimental results demonstrate a 100-fold speedup over state-of-the-art UNNs with robust performance under noise and antenna uncertainties, enabling real-time microwave imaging applications.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.14108v1 公告类型：cross 摘要：由于流体和多孔区域之间的耦合物理现象以及需要在不同的几何形状和边界条件下进行推广，预测穿过多孔体及其周围发生的流动具有挑战性。我们使用两种物理信息学习方法来解决这个问题：物理信息点网（PIPN）和物理信息几何感知神经运算符（P-IGANO）。我们在自由流动区域中强制执行不可压缩的纳维斯托克斯方程，在多孔区域中强制执行 Darcy Forchheimer 扩展，并在统一的损失范围内，并根据几何形状和材料参数调节网络。数据集是使用 OpenFOAM 在包含多孔障碍物的 2D 管道以及具有树冠和建筑物的 3D 防风场景上生成的。我们首先通过制造解决方案的方法验证管道，然后评估对未见过的形状的泛化，对于 PI-GANO，评估对可变边界条件和参数设置的泛化。结果显示，在可见和不可见的情况下，速度和压力误差始终较低，并能准确再现尾流结构。性能下降主要是在尖锐界面附近和梯度较大的区域。总体而言，该研究首次对 PIPN/PI-GANO 对于同步贯通和绕行多孔流进行了系统评估，并显示了它们在无需对每个几何形状进行重新训练的情况下加速设计研究的潜力。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.14108v1 Announce Type: cross Abstract: Predicting flows that occur both through and around porous bodies is challenging due to coupled physics across fluid and porous regions and the need to generalize across diverse geometries and boundary conditions. We address this problem using two Physics Informed learning approaches: Physics Informed PointNets (PIPN) and Physics Informed Geometry Aware Neural Operator (P-IGANO). We enforce the incompressible Navier Stokes equations in the free-flow region and a Darcy Forchheimer extension in the porous region within a unified loss and condition the networks on geometry and material parameters. Datasets are generated with OpenFOAM on 2D ducts containing porous obstacles and on 3D windbreak scenarios with tree canopies and buildings. We first verify the pipeline via the method of manufactured solutions, then assess generalization to unseen shapes, and for PI-GANO, to variable boundary conditions and parameter settings. The results show consistently low velocity and pressure errors in both seen and unseen cases, with accurate reproduction of the wake structures. Performance degrades primarily near sharp interfaces and in regions with large gradients. Overall, the study provides a first systematic evaluation of PIPN/PI-GANO for simultaneous through-and-around porous flows and shows their potential to accelerate design studies without retraining per geometry.

arXiv:2509.23731v2 公告类型：替换 摘要：质子化甲烷（CH5+）是一种高度流动的分子，其氢原子具有较大的空间运动。分子的非简谐效应和氢原子的离域波函数显着影响分子的激发光谱。我们之前为解决分子和固体的振动光谱而开发的神经正则变换（NCT）方法是一种有效处理核量子效应和非谐性的强大方法。使用原子坐标而不是普通坐标中的波函数 NCT，我们成功计算了 CH5+ 的基态和激发态。我们发现基态以及低能和高能激发态的波函数显示出对势能表面上三个驻点的偏好。这项工作扩展了 NCT 方法的适用性，用于计算没有固定几何结构的通量分子的激发态。

English Abstract

arXiv:2509.23731v2 Announce Type: replace Abstract: Protonated methane, CH5+, is a highly fluxional molecule with large spatial motions of the hydrogen atoms. The molecule's anharmonic effects and the delocalized wavefunction of the hydrogen atoms significantly affect the excitation spectrum of the molecule. The neural canonical transformation (NCT) approach, which we previously developed to solve the vibrational spectra of molecules and solids, is a powerful method that effectively treats nuclear quantum effects and anharmonicities. Using NCT with wavefunctions in atomic coordinates rather than normal coordinates, we successfully calculate the ground and excited states of CH5+. We found that the wavefunctions for the ground state, as well as for low- and high-energy excited states, show preferences for the three stationary points on the potential energy surface. This work extends the applicability of the NCT approach for calculating excited states to fluxional molecules without fixed geometry.

arXiv:2511.11968v2 公告类型：替换 摘要：使用物理信息神经网络 (PINN) 导出并评估了轴对称托卡马克几何中高能粒子限制的伴随公式。 PINN 通过使用洛伦兹碰撞算子求解漂移动力学方程的非齐次伴随关系来估计高能离子的平均逃逸时间，从而预测托卡马克几何结构中由于直接离子轨道损失和碰撞传输而导致的快速离子损失。据我们所知，这是首次使用 PINN 来求解托卡马克几何中的漂移动力学方程，这是一个具有挑战性的问题，因为高能离子的快速渡越时间与其缓慢的碰撞时间尺度之间存在较大的时间尺度分离。结果表明，精心设计的 PINN 能够了解大部分血浆体积的平均逃逸时间，这表明了构建快速替代物以在更广泛的优化框架中使用的途径。

English Abstract

arXiv:2511.11968v2 Announce Type: replace Abstract: An adjoint formulation of energetic particle confinement in axisymmetric tokamak geometry is derived and evaluated using a physics-informed neural network (PINN). The PINN estimates the mean escape time of energetic ions by solving an inhomogeneous adjoint of the drift kinetic equation with a Lorentz collision operator, yielding predictions of fast ion loss in tokamak geometry due to direct ion orbit loss and collisional transport. To our knowledge, this is the first time a PINN has been used to solve the drift kinetic equation in tokamak geometry, a challenging problem due to the large time scale separation between the rapid transit time of energetic ions and their slow collisional time scale. It is shown that a careful and intentional design of a PINN is able to learn the mean escape time across the majority of the plasma volume, suggesting a path toward constructing a rapid surrogate for use within a broader optimization framework.

arXiv:2511.21847v2 公告类型：替换 摘要：在这里，我们证明了在液滴形成过程中观察到的随时间演化的界面，以及由此产生的接近夹断的形态，为机器学习 (ML) 框架编码了足够的物理信息，以准确推断关键的流体特性，包括粘度和表面张力。滴落时的液滴快照及其液体特性和流速被用来形成用于训练机器学习算法的数据集。实验包括使用高速成像可视化液滴形成过程并识别最接近破裂的框架。实验是在受控流动条件下使用牛顿流体进行的。就雷诺 (Re) 和 Ohnesorge (Oh) 数而言，我们的条件涵盖范围 0.001< Re< 200 和 0.01 < Oh < 20，使用硅油、乙醇和甘油的水溶液以及甲醇。对于每种情况，都记录了流动参数，以及捕获液滴破碎最后阶段的图像。训练监督回归模型，根据提取的破碎液滴轮廓来预测流体参数。我们的数据集包含 840 个示例。我们的结果表明，夹断时的液滴几何形状包含足够的信息，可以通过机器学习方法推断流体特性。我们的方法可以预测夹断时的表面张力、粘度或液滴形状。这些方法为测量液体特性的传统方法提供了替代方案，同时降低了测量复杂性和评估时间，并有助于集成到自动化中。进行无监督聚类；这些簇代表 Re-Oh 和 Bo-Oh 平面中的区域，表明潜在的表示可能揭示物理特性并提供对液滴动力学的深入了解。

English Abstract

arXiv:2511.21847v2 Announce Type: replace Abstract: Here we demonstrate that the time-evolving interface observed during droplet formation, and consequently the resulting morphology nearing pinch-off, encode sufficient physical information for machine-learning (ML) frameworks to accurately infer key fluid properties, including viscosity and surface tension. Snapshots of dripping drops at the moment of break-up, together with their liquid properties and the flow rate, are used to form a data set for training ML algorithms. Experiments consisted of visualizing, using high-speed imaging, the process of droplet formation and identifying the frame closest to break-up. Experiments were conducted using Newtonian fluids under controlled flow conditions. In terms of the Reynolds (Re) and Ohnesorge (Oh) numbers, our conditions cover the domains 0.001< Re< 200 and 0.01 < Oh < 20, by using silicon oils, aqueous solutions of ethanol and glycerin, and methanol. For each case, flow parameters were recorded, along with images capturing the final stages of droplet break-up. Supervised regression models were trained to predict fluid parameters from the extracted contours of the breaking droplets. Our data set contains 840 examples. Our results demonstrate that the droplet geometry at pinch-off contains sufficient information to infer fluid properties by machine learning approaches. Our methods can predict surface tension, viscosity, or the droplet shape at pinch-off. These approaches provide alternatives to conventional methods to measure liquid properties while reducing measurement complexity and evaluation time and facilitating integration into automation. Unsupervised clustering is performed; the clusters represent regions in the Re-Oh and Bo-Oh planes, indicating that the latent representation may reveal physical properties and offering insight into droplet dynamics.

arXiv:2602.12848v1 公告类型：新 摘要：铜银 (CuAg) 合金由于其高导电性和导热性以及增强的机械强度的独特组合，越来越多地在高性能电气和电子系统中得到应用。然而，对这些合金表面特性如何从根本上影响性能的透彻理解仍然很大程度上不够深入。在这里，我们探索了通过磁控溅射沉积在纹理硅基板上的 Cu、Ag 和 CuAg 薄膜的表面纹理形态、层组成、润湿性和光学特性之间的复杂相互作用。利用数据挖掘和机器学习技术，我们发现了促进 Cassie-Baxter 表面态形成的所有层类型的接触角和表面分形维数之间的强大相关性。我们的分析揭示了层厚度和表面形貌熵亏之间的显着联系，表明金属薄膜生长过程中表面有序/无序的动态演化。此外，我们观察到接触角对层厚度的敏感性暗示着与微观结构演化的相关性。通过K-Means聚类，我们成功地对形成的表面纹理形态进行了分类。最后，开发了随机森林回归模型，仅使用纹理和光学参数即可准确预测水接触角（平均绝对误差约为 5 度）。该模型以及随附的 Python 代码是公开可用的。我们的研究结果为实现定制材料性能的目标表面纹理形态工程建立了一条途径。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.12848v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Copper-silver (CuAg) alloys are increasingly explored for applications in high-performance electrical and electronic systems, owing to their unique combination of high electrical and thermal conductivity and enhanced mechanical strength. Nevertheless, a thorough understanding of how these alloys surface characteristics fundamentally influence properties remains largely underdeveloped. Here, we explored the complex interplay between surface texture morphology, layer composition, wetting, and optical properties of Cu, Ag, and CuAg thin films deposited on textured silicon substrates via magnetron sputtering. Employing data mining and machine learning techniques, we identified robust correlations between contact angle and surface fractal dimension across all layer types promoting Cassie-Baxter surface state formation. Our analysis revealed a significant connection between layer thickness and surface topography entropy deficit, suggesting a dynamic evolution of surface order/disorder during metal film growth. Furthermore, we observed that contact angle sensitivity to layer thickness implied a correlation with microstructure evolution. Through K-Means clustering, we successfully categorized the formed surface textures morphology. Finally, a Random Forest regression model was developed to accurately predict water contact angles (Mean Absolute Error around 5 deg) using only texture and optical parameters. The model, along with accompanying Python code, is publicly available. Our findings establish a pathway towards targeted surface texture morphology engineering for tailored material performance.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.13190v1 公告类型：新 摘要：旋节线分解是材料微观结构形成的关键机制，由于需要准确捕获局部能源景观的无参数方法，长期以来一直对预测建模提出挑战。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种预测旋节线行为的方法，通过对从有限的、小的、代表性的单元计算出的体自由能引入无序粘度校正。我们估算了转变为无序状态所需的能量损失，以实现局部凹形自由能区域的稳定（对于界面形成至关重要），同时抑制长程浓度波动。这种近似规避了界面属性完全从头开始参数化的复杂性，并且非常适合高吞吐量和机器学习框架。我们的方法捕获了支持旋节线动力学的必要物理原理，提供了一种可扩展的途径来预测成分复杂和高熵材料中的旋节线区域。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.13190v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Spinodal decomposition, a key mechanism to microstructure formation in materials, has long posed challenges for predictive modeling, due to the need for parameter-free approaches that accurately capture local energy landscapes. In this work, we propose an approach to predict spinodal behavior by introducing a disorder viscosity correction to bulk free energies computed from finite, small, representative cells. We approximate the energy penalty required to transition into a disordered state to enable the stabilization of locally concave bulk free energy regions - essential for interface formation - while suppressing long-range concentration fluctuations. This approximation circumvents the complexity of full ab initio parameterization of interfacial properties and is well-suited for high-throughput and machine-learning frameworks. Our approach captures the necessary physics underpinning spinodal kinetics, offering a scalable route to predict spinodal regions in compositionally complex and high-entropy materials.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.12294v1 公告类型：交叉 摘要：原子模拟为控制材料行为的物理过程提供了有价值的见解。然而，它们的适用性从根本上受到暴力模拟可访问的有限时间尺度的限制。这一瓶颈通常源于复杂的能源格局，其中系统长时间陷入亚稳态。然而，长期演化是由亚稳态之间的转变控制的，这是罕见的事件并且难以观察。我们提出了一种重要性采样方法，旨在加速马尔可夫链蒙特卡罗（MCMC）模拟的时间尺度。通过采用偏置势，我们的方法增强了对罕见转变事件的采样，同时保留了不同转变路径的相对概率。偏置势由神经网络表示，它实现了高维系统所需的灵活性。我们提出了一个严格的公式，使用从有偏差的模拟中获得的转变路径来获得亚稳态之间的原始转变率。我们进一步使用分支随机游走（BRW）技术来提高效率并减少方差。所提出的方法在 2 维和 14 维系统上进行了验证，证明了其准确性和可扩展性。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.12294v1 Announce Type: cross Abstract: Atomistic simulations provide valuable insights into the physical processes governing material behavior. However, their applicability is fundamentally constrained by the limited time scales accessible to brute-force simulations. This bottleneck often stems from complex energy landscapes where the systems stay trapped in metastable states for long periods of time. Yet, the long-term evolution is controlled by the transitions between the metastable states, which are rare events and difficult to observe. We present an importance sampling method designed to accelerate the time scale of Markov chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) simulations. By employing a bias potential, our approach enhances the sampling of rare transition events while preserving the relative probabilities of distinct transition pathways. The bias potential is represented by a neural network which enables the flexibility needed for high-dimensional systems. We propose a rigorous formulation to obtain the original transition rates between metastable states using transition paths obtained from the biased simulation. We further use a branching random walk (BRW) technique to enhance efficiency and to reduce variance. The proposed methodology is validated on 2-dimensional and 14-dimensional systems, demonstrating its accuracy and scalability.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.12449v1 公告类型：cross 摘要：仅使用足够的统计数据学习吉布斯分布长期以来一直被认为是一个计算难题。另一方面，用于学习吉布斯分布的计算高效算法依赖于对模型生成的完整样本配置的访问。对于物理环境中出现的许多感兴趣的系统，期望观察到完整的样本是不切实际的，因此寻找计算有效的方法来解决仅访问有限的统计数据集的学习问题非常重要。我们使用伊辛模型作为范例，研究了这种情况下计算能力和观察能力之间的权衡。我们证明，通过观察高达 O(γ) 数量级的统计数据，重建具有 ell₁ 宽度 γ 的模型的模型参数是可行的。这种方法使我们能够推断模型的结构并了解其耦合和磁场。我们还讨论了可以获得有关模型结构的先验信息的设置，并表明可以通过更有限的观察能力有效地解决学习问题。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.12449v1 Announce Type: cross Abstract: Learning Gibbs distributions using only sufficient statistics has long been recognized as a computationally hard problem. On the other hand, computationally efficient algorithms for learning Gibbs distributions rely on access to full sample configurations generated from the model. For many systems of interest that arise in physical contexts, expecting a full sample to be observed is not practical, and hence it is important to look for computationally efficient methods that solve the learning problem with access to only a limited set of statistics. We examine the trade-offs between the power of computation and observation within this scenario, employing the Ising model as a paradigmatic example. We demonstrate that it is feasible to reconstruct the model parameters for a model with ell₁ width γ by observing statistics up to an order of O(γ). This approach allows us to infer the model's structure and also learn its couplings and magnetic fields. We also discuss a setting where prior information about structure of the model is available and show that the learning problem can be solved efficiently with even more limited observational power.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.12993v1 公告类型：cross 摘要：神经量子态 (NQS) 为量子化学中的强相关问题提供了灵活且高度表达的波函数参数化。尽管网络架构取得了快速进步，但电子能量的评估仍然几乎完全基于变分蒙特卡罗（VMC）。虽然 VMC 对于自旋链等结构化系统有效，但其电子哈密顿量的准确性和效率受到尖峰分布、随机梯度噪声和样本大小收敛缓慢的阻碍。在这封信中，我们通过将 NQS-VMC 与最近开发的基于 NQS 的选择配置 (NQS-SC) 方法进行比较，评估了 NQS-VMC 有效捕获电子基态相关性的能力。我们对以静态或动态相关性为主的分子系统使用 NQS-VMC 和 NQS-SC 获得的基态优化进行了系统比较。比较表明，NQS-SC 在能量精度和波函数系数方面均优于 NQS-VMC，特别是对于静态相关分子。此外，NQS-SC 表现出强大的系统可改进性，而 NQS-VMC 则不然。这些发现使 NQS-SC 成为取代 NQS-VMC 的电子结构计算的新默认方法。我们进一步观察到，NQS-SC 和 NQS-VMC 都无法有效地捕获动态相关性，这凸显了对未来混合方法的需求，例如建立在 NQS 解决方案之上的多配置扰动理论。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.12993v1 Announce Type: cross Abstract: Neural quantum states (NQS) provide a flexible and highly expressive parameterization of wave functions for strongly correlated problems in quantum chemistry. Despite rapid advances in network architectures, the evaluation of electronic energies remains almost exclusively based on variational Monte Carlo (VMC). While VMC is effective for structured systems such as spin chains, its accuracy and efficiency for electronic Hamiltonians are hindered by sharply peaked distributions, stochastic gradient noise, and slow convergence with sample size. In this letter, we assess the capability of NQS-VMC to efficiently capture correlation in electronic ground states by comparing it to a recently developed NQS-based selected configuration (NQS-SC) approach. We set up a systematic comparison of the ground-state optimizations obtained with NQS-VMC and NQS-SC for molecular systems dominated by either static or dynamical correlation. The comparison demonstrates a clear advantage of NQS-SC over NQS-VMC in both energy accuracy and wave-function coefficients, particularly for statically correlated molecules. Moreover, NQS-SC exhibits robust systematic improvability, whereas NQS-VMC does not. These findings position NQS-SC as the new default approach over NQS-VMC for electronic structure calculations. We further observe that neither NQS-SC nor NQS-VMC can efficiently capture dynamical correlation, highlighting the need for future hybrid methods, such as multiconfigurational perturbation theories built on top of NQS solutions.

中文摘要

arXiv:2602.13187v1 公告类型：cross 摘要：在本文中，我们提出了一种在无相辅助场量子蒙特卡罗（AFQMC）框架内计算精确且可扩展的核力的方法。我们的方法利用能量泛函的自动微分来以与能量评估相当的计算成本获得核梯度。该方法的准确性通过有限差分计算进行了验证，显示出良好的一致性。然后，我们探索了几种用于学习噪声 AFQMC 数据的机器学习 (ML) 策略。这些 ML 势随后用于执行几何优化和微推弹性带 (NEB) 计算，成功识别甲酰胺-甲亚胺酸互变异构的过渡态。由此产生的过渡态几何形状和势垒高度与耦合簇参考值非常一致。这项工作为高精度几何优化、分子动力学或反应路径计算铺平了道路。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.13187v1 Announce Type: cross Abstract: In this article, we present a method for computing accurate and scalable nuclear forces within the phaseless auxiliary-field quantum Monte Carlo (AFQMC) framework. Our approach leverages automatic differentiation of the energy functional to obtain nuclear gradients at a computational cost comparable to that of energy evaluation. The accuracy of the method is validated against finite difference calculations, showing excellent agreement. We then explore several machine learning (ML) strategies for learning noisy AFQMC data. These ML potentials are subsequently used to perform geometry optimizations and nudged elastic band (NEB) calculations, successfully identifying the transition state of the formamide-formimidic acid tautomerization. The resulting transition state geometry and barrier heights are in close agreement with coupled-cluster reference values. This work paves the way for highly accurate geometry optimization, molecular dynamics, or reaction path calculations.

arXiv:2507.17576v2 公告类型：替换 摘要：一碳化铀 (UC) 是一种先进的陶瓷燃料候选者，因为与传统燃料相比，它具有优异的铀密度和导热性。为了在反应堆运行条件下准确建模 UC，我们开发了机器学习原子间势 (MLIP)，使用主动学习程序生成捕获不同原子构型的综合训练数据集。由此产生的 MLIP 可以预测结构、弹性、热物理性质、缺陷形成能和扩散行为，与实验和理论基准很好地吻合。这项工作显着推进了探索 UC 的计算方法，实现了反应堆燃料鉴定所必需的高效大规模和长时间的分子动力学模拟。

English Abstract

arXiv:2507.17576v2 Announce Type: replace Abstract: Uranium monocarbide (UC) is an advanced ceramic fuel candidate due to its superior uranium density and thermal conductivity compared to traditional fuels. To accurately model UC at reactor operating conditions, we developed a machine learning interatomic potential (MLIP) using an active learning procedure to generate a comprehensive training dataset capturing diverse atomic configurations. 中文摘要

arXiv:2602.13092v1 公告类型：新 摘要：我们提出了一种用于动力学等离子体模拟的数值方法，其中相空间分布函数由具有自适应压缩级别的低秩张量网络表示。 Vlasov-Poisson 系统使用斯特朗分裂进行改进，每个子步骤都在相应的变量中进行光谱处理。通过将分布函数和傅里叶变换表示为张量网络对象（状态和算子表示），谱变换以压缩形式直接应用，从而无需重建完整的相空间网格即可实现时间步进。自洽电场也在张量形式中计算。电荷密度是通过收缩速度自由度并提取零傅立叶模式来获得的，这为谱泊松求解器提供了源项。我们在标准基准上验证了该方法，包括朗道阻尼和两流不稳定性。最后，我们系统地研究压缩参数，包括截断公差和内部等级（键合尺寸），如何影响动量和能量守恒、积极行为、丝化鲁棒性和计算成本。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.13092v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: We propose a numerical method for kinetic plasma simulation in which the phase-space distribution function is represented by a low-rank tensor network with an adaptive level of compression. The Vlasov-Poisson system is advanced using Strang splitting, and each substep is treated spectrally in the corresponding variable. By expressing both the distribution function and the Fourier transform as tensor network objects (state and operator representations), spectral transforms are applied directly in compressed form, enabling time stepping without reconstructing the full phase-space grid. The self-consistent electric field is also computed within the tensor formalism. The charge density is obtained by contracting over velocity degrees of freedom and extracting the zero Fourier mode, which provides the source term for a spectral Poisson solver. We validate the approach on standard benchmarks, including Landau damping and the two-stream instability. Finally, we systematically study how compression parameters, including truncation tolerances and internal ranks (bond dimensions), affect momentum and energy conservation, positivity behavior, robustness to filamentation, and computational cost.

阅读原文 ↗
页内定位所在专题
中文摘要

arXiv:2602.13164v1 公告类型：新 摘要：不同动力学状态之间的转换在非平衡系统中普遍存在。作为一个典型的例子，沉积生长通常伴随着不可逆的形态不稳定性。预测从转变前构型的这种转变仍然具有根本性的挑战性，因为早期的前体很弱，空间异质，并且被固有的波动所掩盖。在这里，我们研究了基于二维粒子的电沉积模型中的致密到树枝状转变（CDT），并使用轨迹解析的转变点制定了基于地平线的预警任务。我们证明，预测 CDT 本质上是一个时空问题：无论是静态形态描述符还是单独应用于预定义特征的时间学习都不会产生可靠的预测信号。相比之下，从生长图像中联合优化空间和时间表示的端到端学习可以在广泛的预测范围内实现稳健的预测。对学习到的潜在动力学的分析揭示了低维替代变量的出现，该变量跟踪渐进的形态不稳定并在过渡附近进行重组。我们进一步表明，学习到的时空表示在反应速率条件下表现出有限但系统的可转移性，随着推理条件偏离训练条件，预测性能会下降，这与潜在状态动态的变化一致。总的来说，我们的结果建立了一个预测非平衡界面生长中初期不稳定性的通用公式，对模式形成驱动系统的预测监测和控制具有影响。

English Abstract

arXiv:2602.13164v1 Announce Type: new Abstract: Transitions between distinct dynamical regimes are ubiquitous in nonequilibrium systems. As a prototypical example, deposition growth is often accompanied by irreversible morphological instabilities. Forecasting such transitions from pre-transition configurations remains fundamentally challenging, as early precursors are weak, spatially heterogeneous, and masked by inherent fluctuations. Here, we investigate compact-to-dendritic transitions (CDTs) in a two-dimensional particle-based electrodeposition model and formulate a horizon-based early-warning task using trajectory-resolved transition points. We demonstrate that anticipating the CDT is intrinsically a spatiotemporal problem: neither static morphological descriptors nor temporal learning applied to predefined features alone yields reliable predictive signals. In contrast, end-to-end learning of jointly optimized spatial and temporal representations from growth images enables robust anticipation across a wide range of prediction horizons. Analysis of the learned latent dynamics reveals the emergence of a low-dimensional surrogate variable that tracks progressive morphological destabilization and undergoes reorganization near the transition. We further show that the learned spatiotemporal representation exhibits limited but systematic transferability across reaction-rate conditions, with predictive performance degrading as the inference condition departs from the training condition, consistent with changes in the latent-state dynamics. Overall, our results establish a general formulation for forecasting incipient instabilities in nonequilibrium interfacial growth, with implications for the predictive monitoring and control of pattern-forming driven systems.

页内定位所在专题
中文摘要

arXiv:2510.21767v2 公告类型：替换 摘要：维数灾难在数值和数据驱动方法中普遍存在。这对于同时处理组合时空域的时空方法来说尤其严重。我们研究了量子启发方法在缓解这一诅咒方面的有效性，无论是求解偏微分方程还是进行数据驱动的预测。我们通过在单个矩阵乘积状态（MPS）编码中处理空间和时间维度来实现这一目标。首先，我们对线性和非线性偏微分方程的 MPS 时空求解器进行基准测试，观察到 MPS ansatz 准确地捕获了潜在的时空相关性，同时自由度显着降低。其次，我们开发了一种 MPS-DMD 算法，用于对非线性系统进行准确的长期预测，其运行时间随空间和时间分辨率呈对数缩放。我们还演示了一种应用程序，可以将两种方法结合起来，以廉价且准确的方式预测长期动态。这项研究强调了张量网络在开发有效的、可解释的模型中的作用，这些模型弥合了数值方法和数据驱动方法之间的差距。

English Abstract

arXiv:2510.21767v2 Announce Type: replace Abstract: The curse of dimensionality is ubiquitous in both numerical and data-driven methods. This is particularly severe for space-time methods, which treat the combined space-time domain simultaneously. We investigate the effectiveness of a quantum-inspired approach in alleviating this curse, both for solving PDEs and making data-driven predictions. We achieve this goal by treating both spatial and temporal dimensions within a single matrix product state (MPS) encoding. First, we benchmark our MPS space-time solver for both linear and nonlinear PDEs, observing that the MPS ansatz accurately captures the underlying spatio-temporal correlations while having significantly fewer degrees of freedom. Second, we develop an MPS-DMD algorithm for accurate long-term predictions of nonlinear systems, with runtime scaling logarithmically with both spatial and temporal resolution. We also demonstrate an application where both methods can be combined for cheap and accurate prediction of long-term dynamics. This research highlights the role of tensor networks in developing effective, interpretable models that bridge the gap between numerical methods and data-driven approaches.
